function ItemTable000000_DropItems takes nothing returns nothing
    local widget trigWidget= null
    local unit trigUnit= null
    local integer itemID= 0
    local boolean canDrop= true

    set trigWidget=bj_lastDyingWidget
    if ( trigWidget == null ) then
        set trigUnit=GetTriggerUnit()
    endif

    if ( trigUnit != null ) then
        set canDrop=not IsUnitHidden(trigUnit)
        if ( canDrop and GetChangingUnit() != null ) then
            set canDrop=( GetChangingUnitPrevOwner() == Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE) )
        endif
    endif

    if ( canDrop ) then
        // Item set 0
        call RandomDistReset()
        call RandomDistAddItem('I00L', 80)
        call RandomDistAddItem('I00M', 20)
        set itemID=RandomDistChoose()
        if ( trigUnit != null ) then
            call UnitDropItem(trigUnit, itemID)
        else
            call WidgetDropItem(trigWidget, itemID)
        endif

    endif

    set bj_lastDyingWidget=null
    call DestroyTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
endfunction

            call WidgetDropItem(trigWidget, itemID)
        endif

    endif

    set bj_lastDyingWidget=null
    call DestroyTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
endfunction

function Unit000033_DropItems takes nothing returns nothing
    local widget trigWidget= null
    local unit trigUnit= null
    local integer itemID= 0
    local boolean canDrop= true

    set trigWidget=bj_lastDyingWidget
    if ( trigWidget == null ) then
        set trigUnit=GetTriggerUnit()
    endif

    if ( trigUnit != null ) then
        set canDrop=not IsUnitHidden(trigUnit)
        if ( canDrop and GetChangingUnit() != null ) then
            set canDrop=( GetChangingUnitPrevOwner() == Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE) )
        endif
    endif

    if ( canDrop ) then
        // Item set 0
        call RandomDistReset()
        call RandomDistAddItem('I00N', 30)
        call RandomDistAddItem(- 1, 70)
        set itemID=RandomDistChoose()
        if ( trigUnit != null ) then
            call UnitDropItem(trigUnit, itemID)
        else
            call WidgetDropItem(trigWidget, itemID)
        endif

    endif

    set bj_lastDyingWidget=null
    call DestroyTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
endfunction

function CreateAllDestructables takes nothing returns nothing

    local real life
    set d=CreateDestructable('B000', - 14560.0, 22240.0, 258.000, 0.317, 0)

    call TriggerAddAction(t, function SaveDyingWidget)
    call TriggerAddAction(t, function ItemTable000000_DropItems)

//*
//***************************************************************************

function CreateCameras takes nothing returns nothing

    set gg_cam_Camera_001=CreateCameraSetup()
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_ZOFFSET, 0.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_ROTATION, 88.7, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_ANGLE_OF_ATTACK, 305.3, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_TARGET_DISTANCE, 3215.4, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_ROLL, 0.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_FIELD_OF_VIEW, 70.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_FARZ, 10000.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_NEARZ, 100.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_LOCAL_PITCH, 0.0, 0.0)

    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_LOCAL_ROLL, 0.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetDestPosition(gg_cam_Camera_001, - 5543.6, 25990.9, 0.0)

    set gg_cam_Camera_002=CreateCameraSetup()
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_002, CAMERA_FIELD_ZOFFSET, 0.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_002, CAMERA_FIELD_ROTATION, 0.0, 0.0)

    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_002, CAMERA_FIELD_FARZ, 10000.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_002, CAMERA_FIELD_NEARZ, 100.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_002, CAMERA_FIELD_LOCAL_PITCH, 0.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_002, CAMERA_FIELD_LOCAL_YAW, 0.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_002, CAMERA_FIELD_LOCAL_ROLL, 0.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetDestPosition(gg_cam_Camera_002, - 3157.7, 25702.6, 0.0)

    set gg_cam_ShipCam=CreateCameraSetup()
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_ShipCam, CAMERA_FIELD_ZOFFSET, 0.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_ShipCam, CAMERA_FIELD_ROTATION, 9.9, 0.0)

    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_ShipCam, CAMERA_FIELD_FIELD_OF_VIEW, 70.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_ShipCam, CAMERA_FIELD_FARZ, 4132.2, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_ShipCam, CAMERA_FIELD_NEARZ, 100.0, 0.0)
    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_ShipCam, CAMERA_FIELD_LOCAL_PITCH, 0.0, 0.0)

    call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_ShipCam, CAMERA_FIELD_LOCAL_ROLL, 0.0, 0.0)

    set udg_PlayerGroupRef[5]=bj_FORCE_PLAYER[4]

    set udg_PlayerGroupRef[7]=bj_FORCE_PLAYER[6]

    set udg_PlayerGroupRef[10]=bj_FORCE_PLAYER[9]
    set udg_PlayerGroupRef[11]=bj_FORCE_PLAYER[10]

    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Solar_Flare_Periodic)
endfunction

endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: AntiPersonControl Copy
//===========================================================================
function Trig_AntiPersonControl_Copy_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'H004' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() != udg_PlayerUnitMatch[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitIllusionBJ(GetTriggerUnit()) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_AntiPersonControl_Copy_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() == udg_PlayerUnitMatch[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_AntiPersonControl_Copy_Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() == udg_PlayerUnitMatch[udg_xSpawnNumberLoop] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_AntiPersonControl_Copy_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_AntiPersonControl_Copy_Func001C() ) then
    else
        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))], "TRIGSTR_2218")
    endif
    set udg_xSpawnNumberLoop=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_xSpawnNumberLoop > 12
        if ( Trig_AntiPersonControl_Copy_Func002Func001C() ) then
            set udg_UnitPlayerIteration=udg_xSpawnNumberLoop
            set udg_xSpawnNumberLoop=12
        else
        endif
        set udg_xSpawnNumberLoop=udg_xSpawnNumberLoop + 1
    endloop
    call SetUnitOwner(GetTriggerUnit(), ConvertedPlayer(udg_UnitPlayerIteration), true)
    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))], "TRIGSTR_2219")
    set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))], udg_RandomPositionTarget, 2.00, bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100, 100, 100)
    call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(ConvertedPlayer(udg_UnitPlayerIteration), GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), 0)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_AntiPersonControl_Copy takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, Player(0), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, Player(1), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, Player(2), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, Player(3), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, Player(4), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, Player(5), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, Player(6), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, Player(7), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, Player(8), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, Player(9), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, Player(10), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, Player(11), true)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, Condition(function Trig_AntiPersonControl_Copy_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_AntiPersonControl_Copy, function Trig_AntiPersonControl_Copy_Actions)
endfunction

    call DisplayTimedTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), 5.00, "TRIGSTR_2119")
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Solar Flare Periodic
//
// Put smoke on burning units.
// Add Sound
// Take smoke off dead units?
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func001Func001Func003A takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetUnitLifePercentBJ(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitLifePercent(GetEnumUnit()) - 7.00 ))
    call SetUnitLifeBJ(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetEnumUnit()) - 22.00 ))
    call SetUnitVertexColorBJ(GetEnumUnit(), GetUnitLifePercent(GetEnumUnit()), GetUnitLifePercent(GetEnumUnit()), GetUnitLifePercent(GetEnumUnit()), 0)
    call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", GetEnumUnit(), "SolarSmoke.mdx")
    call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
endfunction

function Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func001Func001Func012Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetRandomInt(1, 2) == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func001Func001Func012C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[1] == udg_SolarFlareTickResetCap[1] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func001Func001Func016C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ActiveRadarTowers >= 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func001Func001Func017C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTriggerEnabled(gg_trg_Perfect_Hearing) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean

        return false
    endif
    return true

        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func001C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func001Func001C() ) then
            set udg_SolarFlareOrigin[1]=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            set udg_SolarFlareTickResetCap[1]=GetRandomInt(133, 533)
            set udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[1]=1
            if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func001Func001Func016C() ) then
                call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(GetPlayersEnemies(udg_AlienPlayer), udg_SolarFlareOrigin[1], ( I2R(udg_SolarFlareTickResetCap[1]) / 6.66 ), bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 70.00, 0.00)
                call DisplayTimedTextToForce(GetPlayersEnemies(udg_AlienPlayer), 2.50, "TRIGSTR_2111")
            else
            endif
            if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func001Func001Func017C() ) then
                call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_AlienTeam, udg_SolarFlareOrigin[1], ( I2R(udg_SolarFlareTickResetCap[1]) / 6.66 ), bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 70.00, 0.00)
                call DisplayTimedTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, 2.50, "TRIGSTR_2112")
            else
            endif
        else
            set udg_RandomPositionTarget=PolarProjectionBJ(udg_SolarFlareOrigin[1], GetRandomReal(0.00, 1300.00), GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(300.00, udg_RandomPositionTarget)
            call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func001Func001Func003A)
            call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
            call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, "Abilities\\Spells\\Human\\FlameStrike\\FlameStrikeEmbers.mdl")
            call BlzSetSpecialEffectScale(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ(), 6.00)
            call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
            call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, "SolarGlare.mdx")
            call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
            call SetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, 'Dlvc', - 1, 2, 0)
            set udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[1]=( udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[1] + 1 )
            if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func001Func001Func012C() ) then
                set udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[1]=0
                if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func001Func001Func012Func002C() ) then
                    set udg_SolarFlareStage=( udg_SolarFlareStage + 1 )
                else
                endif
            else
            endif
        endif
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func002C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func002Func001C() ) then
            set udg_SolarFlareOrigin[2]=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            set udg_SolarFlareTickResetCap[2]=GetRandomInt(133, 533)
            set udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[2]=1
            if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func002Func001Func016C() ) then
                call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(GetPlayersEnemies(udg_AlienPlayer), udg_SolarFlareOrigin[2], ( I2R(udg_SolarFlareTickResetCap[2]) / 6.66 ), bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 70.00, 0.00)
                call DisplayTimedTextToForce(GetPlayersEnemies(udg_AlienPlayer), 2.50, "TRIGSTR_2115")
            else
            endif
            if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func002Func001Func017C() ) then
                call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_AlienTeam, udg_SolarFlareOrigin[2], ( I2R(udg_SolarFlareTickResetCap[2]) / 6.66 ), bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 70.00, 0.00)
                call DisplayTimedTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, 2.50, "TRIGSTR_2116")
            else
            endif
        else
            set udg_RandomPositionTarget=PolarProjectionBJ(udg_SolarFlareOrigin[2], GetRandomReal(0.00, 1300.00), GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(300.00, udg_RandomPositionTarget)
            call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func002Func001Func003A)
            call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
            call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, "Abilities\\Spells\\Human\\FlameStrike\\FlameStrikeEmbers.mdl")
            call BlzSetSpecialEffectScale(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ(), 6.00)
            call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
            call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, "SolarGlare.mdx")
            call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
            call SetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, 'Dlvc', - 1, 2, 0)
            set udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[2]=( udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[2] + 1 )
            if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func002Func001Func012C() ) then
                set udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[2]=0
                if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func002Func001Func012Func002C() ) then
                    set udg_SolarFlareStage=( udg_SolarFlareStage + 1 )
                else
                endif
            else
            endif
        endif
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func003C() ) then
        call ConditionalTriggerExecute(gg_trg_Solar_Flare_Climax)
        if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func003Func002C() ) then
            set udg_SolarFlareOrigin[3]=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            set udg_SolarFlareTickResetCap[3]=GetRandomInt(133, 533)
            set udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[3]=1
            if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func003Func002Func016C() ) then
                call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(GetPlayersEnemies(udg_AlienPlayer), udg_SolarFlareOrigin[3], ( I2R(udg_SolarFlareTickResetCap[3]) / 6.66 ), bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 70.00, 0.00)
                call DisplayTimedTextToForce(GetPlayersEnemies(udg_AlienPlayer), 2.50, "TRIGSTR_2117")
            else
            endif
            if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func003Func002Func017C() ) then
                call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_AlienTeam, udg_SolarFlareOrigin[3], ( I2R(udg_SolarFlareTickResetCap[3]) / 6.66 ), bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 70.00, 0.00)
                call DisplayTimedTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, 2.50, "TRIGSTR_2118")
            else
            endif
        else
            set udg_RandomPositionTarget=PolarProjectionBJ(udg_SolarFlareOrigin[3], GetRandomReal(0.00, 1300.00), GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(275.00, udg_RandomPositionTarget)
            call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func003Func002Func003A)
            call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
            call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, "Abilities\\Spells\\Human\\FlameStrike\\FlameStrikeEmbers.mdl")
            call BlzSetSpecialEffectScale(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ(), 6.00)
            call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
            call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, "SolarGlare.mdx")
            call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
            call SetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, 'Dlvc', - 1, 2, 0)
            set udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[3]=( udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[3] + 1 )
            if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func003Func002Func012C() ) then
                set udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[3]=0
                if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func003Func002Func012Func002C() ) then
                    set udg_SolarFlareStage=( udg_SolarFlareStage + 1 )
                else
                endif
            else
            endif
        endif
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func004C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func004Func001C() ) then
            set udg_SolarFlareOrigin[4]=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            set udg_SolarFlareTickResetCap[4]=GetRandomInt(133, 533)
            set udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[4]=1
            if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func004Func001Func016C() ) then
                call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(GetPlayersEnemies(udg_AlienPlayer), udg_SolarFlareOrigin[4], ( I2R(udg_SolarFlareTickResetCap[4]) / 6.66 ), bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 70.00, 0.00)
                call DisplayTimedTextToForce(GetPlayersEnemies(udg_AlienPlayer), 2.50, "TRIGSTR_2173")
            else
            endif
            if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func004Func001Func017C() ) then
                call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_AlienTeam, udg_SolarFlareOrigin[4], ( I2R(udg_SolarFlareTickResetCap[4]) / 6.66 ), bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 70.00, 0.00)
                call DisplayTimedTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, 2.50, "TRIGSTR_2174")
            else
            endif
        else
            set udg_RandomPositionTarget=PolarProjectionBJ(udg_SolarFlareOrigin[4], GetRandomReal(0.00, 1300.00), GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(275.00, udg_RandomPositionTarget)
            call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func004Func001Func003A)
            call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
            call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, "Abilities\\Spells\\Human\\FlameStrike\\FlameStrikeEmbers.mdl")
            call BlzSetSpecialEffectScale(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ(), 6.00)
            call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
            call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, "SolarGlare.mdx")
            call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
            call SetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, 'Dlvc', - 1, 2, 0)
            set udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[4]=( udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[4] + 1 )
            if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func004Func001Func012C() ) then
                set udg_SolarFlareTickTotal[4]=0
                if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Func004Func001Func012Func002C() ) then
                    set udg_SolarFlareStage=( udg_SolarFlareStage + 1 )
                else
                endif
            else
            endif
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Solar_Flare_Periodic takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Solar_Flare_Periodic=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Solar_Flare_Periodic)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Solar_Flare_Periodic, 0.15)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Solar_Flare_Periodic, function Trig_Solar_Flare_Periodic_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Solar Flare Climax
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_SolarFlareStage == 3 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsTriggerEnabled(GetTriggeringTrigger()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Func008Func001002003 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( IsUnitInGroup(GetEnumUnit(), udg_AllHumansGroup) == true )
endfunction

function Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Func008Func002A takes nothing returns nothing
    call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()))], udg_MeteorStrikePoint, 3.00, bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 100, 0.00)
    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()))], "TRIGSTR_2172")
endfunction

function Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Func008C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ActiveRadarTowers >= 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Func009Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), udg_MeteorStrikePoint) <= 2000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Func009C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTriggerEnabled(gg_trg_Perfect_Hearing) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))], "TRIGSTR_2175")
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Meteors_Apocalyptic)
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Lightning_Apocalyptic)
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Lightning)
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Lightning_Storm)
    if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Func008C() ) then
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocMatching(2000.00, udg_MeteorStrikePoint, Condition(function Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Func008Func001002003))
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Func008Func002A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Func009C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Func009Func001C() ) then
            call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_AlienTeam, udg_MeteorStrikePoint, 3.00, bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 100, 0.00)
            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, "TRIGSTR_2176")
        else
        endif
    else
    endif
    call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Solar_Flare_Climax takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Solar_Flare_Climax=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Solar_Flare_Climax, Condition(function Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Solar_Flare_Climax, function Trig_Solar_Flare_Climax_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Melee Initialization
//
// Default melee game initialization for all players
// Can use a semi-transparent texture for Ice and have the sky set to a space backdrop so that when you move or angle it looks like reflecting ice.
// Make Radio tower (Static Spire) more selectable.
// Make Ambient Map noise ~ mountain (Replace with actual desire)
// Refine ScentSeeker cloud with Rapid spawn, then slower decay. Work on general tooltips some more maybe?
// make Cool Land Fog, pollen in organic area. Alien needs to get abilities over time.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Melee_Initialization_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call EnableDawnDusk(false)
    call VolumeGroupSetVolumeBJ(SOUND_VOLUMEGROUP_AMBIENTSOUNDS, 0.00)
    call SetMapFlag(MAP_FOG_MAP_EXPLORED, true)
    call MeleeStartingVisibility()
    set udg_RocketSoundVariation[1]=gg_snd_NightElf1
    set udg_RocketSoundVariation[2]=gg_snd_NightElf2
    set udg_RocketSoundVariation[3]=gg_snd_NightElf3
    set udg_RocketSoundVariation[4]=gg_snd_NightElfX1
    set udg_AbilityArray[1]='A05L'
    set udg_AbilityArray[2]='A05T'
    set udg_AbilityArray[3]='A012'
    set udg_AbilityArray[4]='A013'
    set udg_AbilityArray[5]='A015'
    set udg_AbilityArray[6]='A016'
    set udg_AbilityArray[7]='A017'
    set udg_AbilityArray[8]='A018'
    set udg_AbilityArray[10]='A01G'
    set udg_AbilityArray[11]='A01I'
    set udg_AbilityArray[12]='A069'
    set udg_AbilityArray[13]='A06Y'
    set udg_AbilityArray[14]='A070'
    set udg_AbilityArray[15]='A07E'
    set udg_ThunderVariable[1]=gg_snd_1Thunder
    set udg_ThunderVariable[2]=gg_snd_2Thunder
    set udg_ThunderVariable[3]=gg_snd_3Thunder
    set udg_ThunderVariable[4]=gg_snd_4Thunder
    set udg_ThunderVariable[5]=gg_snd_5Thunder
    set udg_ThunderVariable[6]=gg_snd_6Thunder
    set udg_ThunderVariable[7]=gg_snd_7Thunder
    // Delete AlienTest preset
    call InitHashtableBJ()
    set udg_VehicleHash=GetLastCreatedHashtableBJ()
    call InitHashtableBJ()
    set udg_ScentSeekerHash=GetLastCreatedHashtableBJ()
    call InitHashtableBJ()
    set udg_VehicleAttackEnabled=GetLastCreatedHashtableBJ()
    call InitHashtableBJ()
    set udg_RocketPairingHash=GetLastCreatedHashtableBJ()
    call InitHashtableBJ()
    set udg_VictoryHash=GetLastCreatedHashtableBJ()
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'h00H', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Shalestorm_Hold_Zone), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_Shalestorm=GetLastCreatedUnit()
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'h00I', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), GetRectCenter(GetPlayableMapRect()), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_RocketBuffer=GetLastCreatedUnit()
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'h00J', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), GetRectCenter(GetPlayableMapRect()), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_RocketBlinderCaster=GetLastCreatedUnit()
    call SetDayNightModels("XenosLightMap.mdx", "XenosLightUnit.mdx")
    // Animate time? Refine alien abilities, make ScentSeeker Alien Visible Only. Give Alien Light, Make Planet Weather. Finish Rocket. Basically done?
    call SetCreepCampFilterState(false)
    call SetCreepCampFilterState(false)
    call EnableMinimapFilterButtons(false, false)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Melee_Initialization takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Melee_Initialization=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Melee_Initialization, function Trig_Melee_Initialization_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Unload
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Unload_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitHiddenBJ(udg_PlayerUnitMatch[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())]) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Unload_Func002A takes nothing returns nothing
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetEnumUnit(), "unload", udg_HumansInFriendlyTanks[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())])
    call SetUnitOwner(udg_HumansInFriendlyTanks[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())], GetTriggerPlayer(), false)
    call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(udg_HumansInFriendlyTanks[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())], GetTriggerPlayer())
    call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer(), GetUnitLoc(udg_HumansInFriendlyTanks[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())]), 0)
endfunction

function Trig_Unload_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TotalTanksGroup, function Trig_Unload_Func002A)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Unload takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Unload=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventEndCinematic(gg_trg_Unload, Player(0))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventEndCinematic(gg_trg_Unload, Player(1))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventEndCinematic(gg_trg_Unload, Player(2))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventEndCinematic(gg_trg_Unload, Player(3))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventEndCinematic(gg_trg_Unload, Player(4))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventEndCinematic(gg_trg_Unload, Player(5))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventEndCinematic(gg_trg_Unload, Player(6))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventEndCinematic(gg_trg_Unload, Player(7))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventEndCinematic(gg_trg_Unload, Player(8))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventEndCinematic(gg_trg_Unload, Player(9))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventEndCinematic(gg_trg_Unload, Player(10))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventEndCinematic(gg_trg_Unload, Player(11))
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Unload, Condition(function Trig_Unload_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Unload, function Trig_Unload_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Index Tank Sharers
//
// Make it so when a unit clicks rocket if its a human it gives rocket to that human then back to its other owner.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Index_Tank_Sharers_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitUserData(GetOrderTargetUnit()) >= 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'H004' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitIllusionBJ(GetTriggerUnit()) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() == udg_PlayerUnitMatch[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()) != GetOwningPlayer(GetOrderTargetUnit()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetOrderTargetUnit()) != 'h00E' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetOrderTargetUnit()) != 'h00F' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetOrderTargetUnit()) != 'u002' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitCurrentOrder(GetTriggerUnit()) == String2OrderIdBJ("smart") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Index_Tank_Sharers_Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()) != GetOwningPlayer(GetOrderTargetUnit()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Index_Tank_Sharers_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), GetUnitLoc(GetOrderTargetUnit())) <= 275.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Index_Tank_Sharers_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Index_Tank_Sharers_Func001C() ) then
        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))], "TRIGSTR_2094")
        set udg_HumansInFriendlyTanks[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=GetOrderedUnit()
        call SetUnitOwner(GetTriggerUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetOrderTargetUnit()), false)
    else
        if ( Trig_Index_Tank_Sharers_Func001Func002C() ) then
            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))], "TRIGSTR_2076")
        else
        endif
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Index_Tank_Sharers takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Index_Tank_Sharers=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Index_Tank_Sharers, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ISSUED_TARGET_ORDER)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Index_Tank_Sharers, Condition(function Trig_Index_Tank_Sharers_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Index_Tank_Sharers, function Trig_Index_Tank_Sharers_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: PhD
//
// Set all portions of the message to the same dissolve rate. (duration)
//===========================================================================
function Trig_PhD_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A069' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_PhD_Func001Func002001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetFilterPlayer() != udg_AlienPlayer )
endfunction

function Trig_PhD_Func001Func003Func001001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetFilterPlayer() != udg_AlienPlayer )
endfunction

function Trig_PhD_Func001Func004001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetFilterPlayer() != udg_AlienPlayer )
endfunction

function Trig_PhD_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_PhDUseable == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_PhD_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_PhD_Func001C() ) then
        call DisplayTimedTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))], 10.00, "TRIGSTR_2019")
    else
        call DisplayTimedTextToForce(GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_PhD_Func001Func002001001)), 10.00, ( "Biology Report: (Prepared by: " + ( GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())) + ")" ) ))
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > udg_PHdNumber
            call DisplayTimedTextToForce(GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_PhD_Func001Func003Func001001001)), 10.00, udg_PHdTrackedAbilities[udg_GenericLoopCount])
            set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
        endloop
        call DisplayTimedTextToForce(GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_PhD_Func001Func004001001)), 10.00, ( "Alien Health: " + R2S(GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, udg_AlienUnit)) ))
        set udg_PhDUseable=1
        call TriggerSleepAction(55.00)
        set udg_PhDUseable=0
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_PhD takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_PhD=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_PhD, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_PhD, Condition(function Trig_PhD_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_PhD, function Trig_PhD_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Salvage
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Salvage_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A070' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Salvage_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_RandomInteger <= 7 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Salvage_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_RandomInteger=GetRandomInt(1, 8)
    if ( Trig_Salvage_Func002C() ) then
        call SetPlayerStateBJ(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD, ( GetPlayerState(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD) + 1 ))
        call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_2057", GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), 150.00, 7.50, 100, 100, 100, 0)
        call SetTextTagPermanentBJ(GetLastCreatedTextTag(), false)
        call SetTextTagFadepointBJ(GetLastCreatedTextTag(), 1.00)
        call SetTextTagLifespanBJ(GetLastCreatedTextTag(), 2.00)
    else
        call SetPlayerStateBJ(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER, ( GetPlayerState(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER) + 1 ))
        call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_2061", GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), 150.00, 7.50, 100, 100, 100, 0)
        call SetTextTagPermanentBJ(GetLastCreatedTextTag(), false)
        call SetTextTagFadepointBJ(GetLastCreatedTextTag(), 1.00)
        call SetTextTagLifespanBJ(GetLastCreatedTextTag(), 2.00)
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Salvage takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Salvage=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Salvage, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_CAST)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Salvage, Condition(function Trig_Salvage_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Salvage, function Trig_Salvage_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Scorpion Sting Initiation
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Scorpion_Sting_Initiation_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( 'n005' == GetUnitTypeId(GetAttacker()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()) == Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetAttacker(), "thunderbolt", GetAttackedUnitBJ())
    call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
    call TriggerSleepAction(85.00)
    call EnableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Hydra Attack
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Hydra_Attack_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( 'n004' == GetUnitTypeId(GetAttackedUnitBJ()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetAttackedUnitBJ()) == Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Hydra_Attack_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(udg_HydraUnit) == Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Hydra_Attack_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetUnitOwner(udg_HydraUnit, Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), false)
    call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
    call TriggerSleepAction(25.00)
    call EnableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
    if ( Trig_Hydra_Attack_Func005C() ) then
        call SetUnitOwner(udg_HydraUnit, Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), false)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Hydra_Attack takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Hydra_Attack=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Hydra_Attack, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ATTACKED)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Hydra_Attack, Condition(function Trig_Hydra_Attack_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Hydra_Attack, function Trig_Hydra_Attack_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function Trig_Meteor_Toss_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSpellTargetUnit()) == 'o001' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSpellTargetUnit()) == 'o000' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSpellTargetUnit()) == 'o002' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSpellTargetUnit()) == 'u001' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSpellTargetUnit()) == 'u000' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Meteor_Toss_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetAbilityName(GetSpellAbilityId()), 1, 6) == "Meteor" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not Trig_Meteor_Toss_Func005C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Meteor_Toss_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'h009', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "shadowstrike", GetSpellTargetUnit())
    call RemoveUnit(GetLastCreatedUnit())
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Psychic Shriek
//
// Psychic Barrage should reveal area.
// Nerf Turrets?
// Add Boulder Toss ability?
// Adjust polymer to occur more frequently but also have stuff cost more?
// Add more neutral aliens
// Give alien faster attacks
// Spellbook hide abilities?
// Make Echolocation default?
// Fix camouflage description typo
// Make rocket fly again (movespeed issue) (maybe change acelerator?)
// Remove some leaks?
// Fix Robot Icon
// Fix Broken Terrain, boundaries and Doodad hiding?
// Fix Scentseeker to not suck.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetAbilityName(GetSpellAbilityId()), 1, 18) == "Alien, Psychic Shr" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Func012Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE) != true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_MECHANICAL) != true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitHiddenBJ(GetEnumUnit()) != true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetEnumUnit() != udg_AlienUnit ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Func012A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Func012Func001C() ) then
        call SetUnitLifePercentBJ(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitLifePercent(GetEnumUnit()) - 10.00 ))
        call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit())), GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect()), 1, bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_FLASHY, GetRandomReal(0, 100.00), GetRandomReal(0, 100.00), GetRandomReal(0, 100.00))
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_PsychicShriekZone=GetSpellTargetLoc()
    call CreateFogModifierRadiusLocBJ(true, udg_AlienPlayer, FOG_OF_WAR_VISIBLE, udg_PsychicShriekZone, 150.00)
    set udg_ShriekVisibility=GetLastCreatedFogModifier()
    set udg_AlienCaster=GetTriggerUnit()
    call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", GetTriggerUnit(), "PsychicChannel.mdx")
    set udg_PsychicBarrageSFX[3]=GetLastCreatedEffectBJ()
    call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetSpellTargetLoc(), "Psychic Shriek.mdx")
    set udg_PsychicBarrageSFX[4]=GetLastCreatedEffectBJ()
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Psychic_Shriek_Loop)
    // Additional new Upfront Damage for Psychic Shriek
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(150.00, udg_PsychicShriekZone)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Func012A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Psychic_Shriek takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Psychic_Shriek=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Psychic_Shriek, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Psychic_Shriek, Condition(function Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Psychic_Shriek, function Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Psychic Barrage
//
// Psychic Barrage should reveal area.
// Nerf Turrets?
// Add Boulder Toss ability?
// Adjust polymer to occur more frequently but also have stuff cost more?
// Add more neutral aliens
// Give alien faster attacks
// Spellbook hide abilities?
// Make Echolocation default?
// Fix camouflage description typo
// Make rocket fly again (movespeed issue) (maybe change acelerator?)
// Remove some leaks?
// Fix Robot Icon
// Fix Broken Terrain, boundaries and Doodad hiding?
// Fix Scentseeker to not suck.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Psychic_Barrage_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetAbilityName(GetSpellAbilityId()), 1, 18) == "Alien, Psychic Bar" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Psychic_Barrage_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_PsychicBarrageZone=GetSpellTargetLoc()
    call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_AlienSound, 100, udg_PsychicBarrageZone, 0)
    call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_RockHeavyBashStone1, 100, udg_PsychicBarrageZone, 0)
    call CreateFogModifierRadiusLocBJ(true, udg_AlienPlayer, FOG_OF_WAR_VISIBLE, udg_PsychicBarrageZone, 650.00)
    set udg_BarrageVisibility=GetLastCreatedFogModifier()
    set udg_AlienCaster=GetTriggerUnit()
    call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", GetTriggerUnit(), "PsychicChannel.mdx")
    set udg_PsychicBarrageSFX[1]=GetLastCreatedEffectBJ()
    call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetSpellTargetLoc(), "Psychic Barrage.mdx")
    set udg_PsychicBarrageSFX[2]=GetLastCreatedEffectBJ()
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Psychic_Barrage_Loop)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Psychic_Barrage takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Psychic_Barrage=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Psychic_Barrage, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Psychic_Barrage, Condition(function Trig_Psychic_Barrage_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Psychic_Barrage, function Trig_Psychic_Barrage_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Psychic Barrage Loop
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Psychic_Barrage_Loop_Func001Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE) != true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_MECHANICAL) != true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitHiddenBJ(GetEnumUnit()) != true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetEnumUnit() != udg_AlienUnit ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Psychic_Barrage_Loop_Func001Func002A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Psychic_Barrage_Loop_Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
        call SetUnitLifePercentBJ(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitLifePercent(GetEnumUnit()) - 0.50 ))
        call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit())), GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect()), 1, bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_FLASHY, GetRandomReal(0, 100.00), GetRandomReal(0, 100.00), GetRandomReal(0, 100.00))
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Psychic_Barrage_Loop_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitCurrentOrder(udg_AlienCaster) == String2OrderIdBJ("carrionswarm") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Psychic_Barrage_Loop_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Psychic_Barrage_Loop_Func001C() ) then
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(650.00, udg_PsychicBarrageZone)
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Psychic_Barrage_Loop_Func001Func002A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    else
        call DestroyEffectBJ(udg_PsychicBarrageSFX[1])
        call DestroyEffectBJ(udg_PsychicBarrageSFX[2])
        call DestroyFogModifier(udg_BarrageVisibility)
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Psychic_Barrage_Loop takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Psychic_Barrage_Loop=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Psychic_Barrage_Loop)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Psychic_Barrage_Loop, 0.10)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Psychic_Barrage_Loop, function Trig_Psychic_Barrage_Loop_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Psychic Shriek Loop
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Loop_Func001Func003Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE) != true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_MECHANICAL) != true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitHiddenBJ(GetEnumUnit()) != true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetEnumUnit() != udg_AlienUnit ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Loop_Func001Func003A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Loop_Func001Func003Func001C() ) then
        call SetUnitLifePercentBJ(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitLifePercent(GetEnumUnit()) - 1.00 ))
        call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit())), GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect()), 1, bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_FLASHY, GetRandomReal(0, 100.00), GetRandomReal(0, 100.00), GetRandomReal(0, 100.00))
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Loop_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_PsychicShriekDuration <= 3.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Loop_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Loop_Func001C() ) then
        set udg_PsychicShriekDuration=( udg_PsychicShriekDuration + 0.10 )
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(150.00, udg_PsychicShriekZone)
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Loop_Func001Func003A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    else
        call DestroyEffectBJ(udg_PsychicBarrageSFX[3])
        call DestroyEffectBJ(udg_PsychicBarrageSFX[4])
        call DestroyFogModifier(udg_BarrageVisibility)
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
        set udg_PsychicShriekDuration=0.00
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Psychic_Shriek_Loop takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Psychic_Shriek_Loop=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Psychic_Shriek_Loop)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Psychic_Shriek_Loop, 0.10)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Psychic_Shriek_Loop, function Trig_Psychic_Shriek_Loop_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Pounce
//
// Pounce: You drew in the jump to target distance by 60. Its currently 20, it used to be 80 if you want to change it back.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Pounce_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetAbilityName(GetSpellAbilityId()), 1, 10) == "Alien, Pou" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Pounce_Func013C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_AlienJumpIndex == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Pounce_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'h00D', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(3.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "thunderbolt", GetSpellTargetUnit())
    set udg_AlienJumpIndex=( udg_AlienJumpIndex + 1 )
    set udg_AlienJumpPoint[udg_AlienJumpIndex]=PolarProjectionBJ(GetSpellTargetLoc(), 20.00, AngleBetweenPoints(GetSpellTargetLoc(), GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienJumping[udg_AlienJumpIndex])))
    set udg_AlienJumping[udg_AlienJumpIndex]=GetSpellAbilityUnit()
    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('Arav', udg_AlienJumping[udg_AlienJumpIndex])
    set udg_AlienParabolicExpanseStartEnd[udg_AlienJumpIndex]=DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienJumping[udg_AlienJumpIndex]), udg_AlienJumpPoint[udg_AlienJumpIndex])
    set udg_AlienParabolicFocus[udg_AlienJumpIndex]=( DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienJumping[udg_AlienJumpIndex]), udg_AlienJumpPoint[udg_AlienJumpIndex]) / 2.00 )
    call TriggerSleepAction(0.50)
    call SetUnitPathing(udg_AlienJumping[udg_AlienJumpIndex], false)
    if ( Trig_Pounce_Func013C() ) then
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Pounce_Loop)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Pounce takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Pounce=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Pounce, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Pounce, Condition(function Trig_Pounce_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Pounce, function Trig_Pounce_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Pounce Loop
//
// Create a Generic Grenade Loop with Very flexible variables to enable Grenade-type Spells.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Pounce_Loop_Func001Func001Func010C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_AlienJumpIndex == 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Pounce_Loop_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienJumping[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount]), udg_AlienJumpPoint[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount]) <= 15.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Pounce_Loop_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount > udg_AlienJumpIndex
        if ( Trig_Pounce_Loop_Func001Func001C() ) then
            call SetUnitPathing(udg_AlienJumping[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount], true)
            call SetUnitFlyHeightBJ(udg_AlienJumping[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount], 0.00, 10000.00)
            call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('Arav', udg_AlienJumping[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount])
            set udg_AlienJumping[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount]=udg_AlienJumping[udg_AlienJumpIndex]
            set udg_AlienJumpIndex=( udg_AlienJumpIndex - 1 )
            set udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount=( udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount - 1 )
            if ( Trig_Pounce_Loop_Func001Func001Func010C() ) then
                call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
            else
            endif
        else
            call SetUnitPositionLoc(udg_AlienJumping[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount], PolarProjectionBJ(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienJumping[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount]), 15.00, AngleBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienJumping[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount]), udg_AlienJumpPoint[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount])))
            call SetUnitFlyHeightBJ(udg_AlienJumping[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount], ( 1.00 * SquareRoot(( Pow(udg_AlienParabolicFocus[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount], 2.00) - Pow(( DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienJumping[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount]), udg_AlienJumpPoint[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount]) - udg_AlienParabolicFocus[udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount] ), 2.00) )) ), 10000.00)
        endif
        set udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount=udg_zSpiderJumpLoopCount + 1
    endloop
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Pounce_Loop takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Pounce_Loop=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Pounce_Loop)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Pounce_Loop, 0.01)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Pounce_Loop, function Trig_Pounce_Loop_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Sting_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean

        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Sting_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetUnitTimeScalePercent(GetTriggerUnit(), 180.00)
    set udg_StingVictim=GetSpellTargetUnit()
    call TriggerSleepAction(0.62)
    call SetUnitTimeScalePercent(GetTriggerUnit(), 100.00)
    call SetUnitMoveSpeed(udg_StingVictim, ( GetUnitDefaultMoveSpeed(udg_StingVictim) / 4.00 ))
    call TriggerSleepAction(1.00)
    call SetUnitMoveSpeed(udg_StingVictim, ( GetUnitDefaultMoveSpeed(udg_StingVictim) / 2.00 ))
    call TriggerSleepAction(3.75)
    call SetUnitMoveSpeed(udg_StingVictim, GetUnitDefaultMoveSpeed(udg_StingVictim))
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Tunnel
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Tunnel_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A002' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Tunnel_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTerrainPathableBJ(udg_TunnelDestination, PATHING_TYPE_FLYABILITY) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Tunnel_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TunnelDestination=GetSpellTargetLoc()
    if ( Trig_Tunnel_Func002C() ) then
        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, "TRIGSTR_1265")
        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A002', GetTriggerUnit())
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A002', GetTriggerUnit())
        call TriggerSleepAction(1.00)
        call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(udg_AlienUnit, "move", udg_TunnelDestination)
        call IssueImmediateOrderBJ(udg_AlienUnit, "stop")
    else
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(PolarProjectionBJ(GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), 250.00, AngleBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), GetSpellTargetLoc())), "DigDark.mdx")
        set udg_TunnelFX[1]=GetLastCreatedEffectBJ()
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetSpellTargetLoc(), "DigDark.mdx")
        set udg_TunnelFX[2]=GetLastCreatedEffectBJ()
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetSpellTargetLoc(), "Objects\\Spawnmodels\\Undead\\ImpaleTargetDust\\ImpaleTargetDust.mdl")
        set udg_TunnelFX[3]=GetLastCreatedEffectBJ()
        call TriggerSleepAction(3.75)
        call DestroyEffectBJ(udg_TunnelFX[1])
        call DestroyEffectBJ(udg_TunnelFX[2])
        call DestroyEffectBJ(udg_TunnelFX[3])
        call SetUnitPositionLoc(udg_AlienUnit, udg_TunnelDestination)
        call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(udg_AlienPlayer, GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), 0)
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), "NewDirtEXNofire.mdx")
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Tunnel takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Tunnel=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Tunnel, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_CAST)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Tunnel, Condition(function Trig_Tunnel_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Tunnel, function Trig_Tunnel_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Func001Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(udg_AlienUnit, 'BOwk') == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Func001Func002Func007C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(udg_AlienUnit, 'BOwk') == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTriggerEnabled(gg_trg_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Damage) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Func001Func004Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTriggerEnabled(gg_trg_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Damage) != true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Func001Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_MirrorskinAmbushCounter >= 30 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(udg_AlienUnit, 'BOwk') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitCurrentOrder(udg_AlienUnit) == String2OrderIdBJ("") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Func001C() ) then
        set udg_MirrorskinAmbushCounter=( udg_MirrorskinAmbushCounter + 1 )
        if ( Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Func001Func004C() ) then
            if ( Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Func001Func004Func001C() ) then
                call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Damage)
                call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("overhead", udg_AlienUnit, "Abilities\\Spells\\Undead\\Curse\\CurseTarget.mdl")
                set udg_MirrorSkinAmbushDmgEffect=GetLastCreatedEffectBJ()
            else
            endif
        else
            call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Damage)
        endif
    else
        if ( Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Func001Func002C() ) then
            call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
            call TriggerSleepAction(0.50)
            call EnableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
            set udg_MirrorskinAmbushCounter=0
            call DestroyEffectBJ(udg_MirrorSkinAmbushDmgEffect)
            if ( Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Func001Func002Func007C() ) then
                call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
            else
            endif
        else
            if ( Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
                call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
            else
            endif
            set udg_MirrorskinAmbushCounter=0
            call DestroyEffectBJ(udg_MirrorSkinAmbushDmgEffect)
        endif
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_MirrorSkin_Ambush takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_MirrorSkin_Ambush=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_MirrorSkin_Ambush)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_MirrorSkin_Ambush, 0.10)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_MirrorSkin_Ambush, function Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: MirrorSkin Ambush Damage
//===========================================================================
function Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Damage_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetAttacker()) == 'H005' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetAttackedUnitBJ(), UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Damage_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_MirrorskinAmbushCounter=0
    call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
    call UnitDamageTargetBJ(udg_AlienUnit, GetAttackedUnitBJ(), 200.00, ATTACK_TYPE_CHAOS, DAMAGE_TYPE_NORMAL)
    call DestroyEffectBJ(udg_MirrorSkinAmbushDmgEffect)
    call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_1624", GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), 200.00, 10, 100, 100, 100, 0)
    call SetTextTagPermanentBJ(GetLastCreatedTextTag(), false)
    call SetTextTagFadepointBJ(GetLastCreatedTextTag(), 1.00)
    call SetTextTagLifespanBJ(GetLastCreatedTextTag(), 3.50)
endfunction

    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Damage, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ATTACKED)

    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Damage, function Trig_MirrorSkin_Ambush_Damage_Actions)
endfunction

endfunction

endfunction

function Trig_Marine_Learn_First_Ability_Func016001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( SubStringBJ(GetAbilityName(GetSpellAbilityId()), 1, 5) == "Learn" )
endfunction

function Trig_Marine_Learn_First_Ability_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A00J') ) then // INLINED!!
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A00B', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A00G') ) then // INLINED!!
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A00D', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A00H') ) then // INLINED!!
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A00C', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A00I') ) then // INLINED!!
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A00F', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A00I') ) then // INLINED!!
        call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_ExhaustSynthesisBonus)
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A00K') ) then // INLINED!!
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A00E', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A00L') ) then // INLINED!!
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A00A', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A068') ) then // INLINED!!
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A067', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A068') ) then // INLINED!!
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('Reuv', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A06A') ) then // INLINED!!
        call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED)
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A06A') ) then // INLINED!!
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R001', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A06A') ) then // INLINED!!
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A06B', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A06C') ) then // INLINED!!
        call SetPlayerStateBJ(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_FOOD_CAP, ( GetPlayerState(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_FOOD_CAP) + 10 ))
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A06C') ) then // INLINED!!
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A06D', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetAbilityName(GetSpellAbilityId()), 1, 5) == "Learn") ) then // INLINED!!
        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A00M', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
        // n
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Marine_Learn_First_Ability takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Marine_Learn_First_Ability=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Marine_Learn_First_Ability, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Marine_Learn_First_Ability, Condition(function Trig_Marine_Learn_First_Ability_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Marine_Learn_First_Ability, function Trig_Marine_Learn_First_Ability_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Func027001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( SubStringBJ(udg_AbilityCastString, 1, 5) == "Learn" )
endfunction

function Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Func028001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( SubStringBJ(udg_AbilityCastString, 1, 5) == "Learn" )
endfunction

function Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Func029001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( SubStringBJ(udg_AbilityCastString, 1, 5) == "Learn" )
endfunction

function Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Func030C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(udg_AbilityCastString, 1, 5) == "Learn" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerState(udg_AlienPlayer, PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER) >= 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Func031C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(udg_AbilityCastString, 1, 5) == "Learn" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_AlienLearnedActiveAbilities == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_PassiveAbilityLearned != "yes" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_AbilityCastString=GetAbilityName(GetSpellAbilityId())
    if ( Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Func002C() ) then
        set udg_PHdNumber=( udg_PHdNumber + 1 )
        set udg_PHdTrackedAbilities[udg_PHdNumber]="Dimensional Rifter (Target Resistant)"
        if ( (udg_AlienLearnedActiveAbilities != 0) ) then // INLINED!!
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A027', GetTriggerUnit())
        else
            // n
        endif
        set udg_PassiveAbilityLearned="yes"
        call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A01U', udg_AlienPlayer)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Func003C() ) then
        set udg_PHdNumber=( udg_PHdNumber + 1 )
        set udg_PHdTrackedAbilities[udg_PHdNumber]="Anodized Claws (Tank slow, passive)"
        if ( (udg_AlienLearnedActiveAbilities != 0) ) then // INLINED!!
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A04J', GetTriggerUnit())
        else
            // n
        endif
        set udg_PassiveAbilityLearned="yes"
        call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A056', udg_AlienPlayer)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Func004C() ) then

        set udg_PHdTrackedAbilities[udg_PHdNumber]="Darklight (Spy orb)"
        if ( (udg_AlienLearnedActiveAbilities == 0) ) then // INLINED!!
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A05U', GetTriggerUnit())
        else
            // n
        endif
        set udg_AlienLearnedActiveAbilities=( udg_AlienLearnedActiveAbilities + 1 )
        if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(), udg_AlienTeam) then
        set udg_DarklightSound=gg_snd_WispWhat3
        endif
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Reform_Darklight)
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Darklight_Found_Victim)
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_AutoWander_Toggle)
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Refocus_Darklight)
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Spawn_Darklight)
        call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(true, 'A061', udg_AlienPlayer)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Func025C() ) then
        set udg_PHdNumber=( udg_PHdNumber + 1 )
        set udg_PHdTrackedAbilities[udg_PHdNumber]="Listen to Fear (Can hear nearby humans)"
        if ( (udg_AlienLearnedActiveAbilities == 0) ) then // INLINED!!
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A04K', GetTriggerUnit())
        else
            // n
        endif
        set udg_AlienLearnedActiveAbilities=( udg_AlienLearnedActiveAbilities + 1 )
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Listen_To_Fear)
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A02G', GetTriggerUnit())
        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A02K', GetTriggerUnit())
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Alien_Add_Abilities)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Func026C() ) then
        set udg_PHdNumber=( udg_PHdNumber + 1 )
        set udg_PHdTrackedAbilities[udg_PHdNumber]="Scent Seeker (Can track human scents)"
        if ( (udg_AlienLearnedActiveAbilities == 0) ) then // INLINED!!
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A040', GetTriggerUnit())
        else
            // n
        endif
        set udg_AlienLearnedActiveAbilities=( udg_AlienLearnedActiveAbilities + 1 )
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_ScentSeeker_Fog)
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_ActivateAlienScentSeeker)
        call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_ActivateAlienScentSeeker)
    else
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(udg_AbilityCastString, 1, 5) == "Learn") ) then // INLINED!!
        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A02G', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(udg_AbilityCastString, 1, 5) == "Learn") ) then // INLINED!!
        call SetUnitMoveSpeed(udg_AlienUnit, ( GetUnitDefaultMoveSpeed(udg_AlienUnit) + ( 3.00 * I2R(udg_PHdNumber) ) ))
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(udg_AbilityCastString, 1, 5) == "Learn") ) then // INLINED!!
        call SetPlayerStateBJ(udg_AlienPlayer, PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER, ( GetPlayerState(udg_AlienPlayer, PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER) - 1 ))
    else
        // n
    endif
    if ( Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Func030C() ) then
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A02G', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Func031C() ) then
        call SetPlayerStateBJ(udg_AlienPlayer, PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER, ( GetPlayerState(udg_AlienPlayer, PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER) + 1 ))
        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, "TRIGSTR_1643")
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A02G', GetTriggerUnit())
        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A02K', GetTriggerUnit())
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Alien_Add_Abilities)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES, Condition(function Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES, function Trig_ALIEN_Learns_ABILITIES_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: PEDD AutoLoad
//
// You can make a trigger that adds PEDDs to a group, then when a unit is issued an order it checks the PEDD group, if active to see if that players owner owns a PEDD with an Unhidden Marine, if so blow up PEDD
//===========================================================================
function Trig_PEDD_AutoLoad_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSummonedUnit()) == 'u003' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_PEDD_AutoLoad_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetSummoningUnit(), "smart", GetSummonedUnit())
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetSummonedUnit(), "load", GetSummoningUnit())
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_PEDD_AutoLoad takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_PEDD_AutoLoad=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_PEDD_AutoLoad, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SUMMON)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_PEDD_AutoLoad, Condition(function Trig_PEDD_AutoLoad_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_PEDD_AutoLoad, function Trig_PEDD_AutoLoad_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: PEDD Destroy
//===========================================================================
function Trig_PEDD_Destroy_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'u003' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetAbilityName(GetSpellAbilityId()), 1, 6) == "Unload" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_PEDD_Destroy_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call KillUnit(GetTriggerUnit())
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_PEDD_Destroy takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_PEDD_Destroy=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_PEDD_Destroy, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_ENDCAST)
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_PEDD_Destroy, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_CAST)
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_PEDD_Destroy, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_PEDD_Destroy, Condition(function Trig_PEDD_Destroy_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_PEDD_Destroy, function Trig_PEDD_Destroy_Actions)
endfunction

    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_Drill_and_Dig_Site_Info, Player(5), true)

    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_Drill_and_Dig_Site_Info, Player(7), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_Drill_and_Dig_Site_Info, Player(8), true)
