//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Drill Teleport
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Drill_Teleport_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetAbilityName(GetSpellAbilityId()), 1, 5) == "Drill" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSpellTargetUnit()) == 'h00B' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Drill_Teleport_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetEnumUnit() != GetSpellTargetUnit() ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_MANA, GetEnumUnit()) == GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_MANA, GetSpellTargetUnit()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Drill_Teleport_Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Drill_Teleport_Func001Func001C() ) then
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), "Abilities\\Weapons\\AncientProtectorMissile\\AncientProtectorMissile.mdl")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
        call SetUnitPositionLoc(GetTriggerUnit(), GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit()))
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), "Abilities\\Weapons\\AncientProtectorMissile\\AncientProtectorMissile.mdl")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
        call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), 0)
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Drill_Teleport_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll('h00B'), function Trig_Drill_Teleport_Func001A)
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Drill_Teleport=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Drill_Teleport, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Drill_Teleport, Condition(function Trig_Drill_Teleport_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Drill_Teleport, function Trig_Drill_Teleport_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Drill Refund
//
// Drill cooldown was 70 sec.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Drill_Refund_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetAbilityName(GetSpellAbilityId()), 1, 5) == "Drill" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSpellTargetUnit()) == 'h00C' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Drill_Refund_Func003Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_GenericLoopCount)) == 'I002' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Drill_Refund_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))], "TRIGSTR_2149")
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > 6
        if ( Trig_Drill_Refund_Func003Func001C() ) then
            call SetItemCharges(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_PlayerUnitMatch[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())], udg_GenericLoopCount), ( GetItemCharges(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_PlayerUnitMatch[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())], udg_GenericLoopCount)) + 1 ))
            return
        else
        endif
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
endfunction

function InitTrig_Drill_Refund takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Drill_Refund=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Drill_Refund, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Drill_Refund, Condition(function Trig_Drill_Refund_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Drill_Refund, function Trig_Drill_Refund_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice_Func002001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00C' )
endfunction

function Trig_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice_Func002002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00B' )
endfunction

function Trig_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not GetBooleanOr((GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00C'), (GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00B')) ) then // INLINED!!
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_MANA, GetEnumUnit()) == GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_MANA, GetTriggerUnit()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice_Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice_Func001Func001C() ) then
        call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())], GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit()), 1.50, bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 50.00, 100, 0.00)
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll(GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit())), function Trig_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice_Func001A)
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice=CreateTrigger()

    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice, Player(1), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice, Player(2), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice, Player(3), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice, Player(4), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice, Player(5), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice, Player(6), true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ(gg_trg_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice, Player(7), true)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice, Condition(function Trig_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice, function Trig_Dig_and_Drill_Location_Notice_Actions)
endfunction

    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetAbilityName(GetSpellAbilityId()), 1, 10) == "Alien, Dig" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(udg_DigSiteUnit) == 'h00C' ) ) then
        return false

    return true

    if ( not ( GetEnumUnit() != udg_DigSiteUnit ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_MANA, GetEnumUnit()) == GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_MANA, udg_DigSiteUnit) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Dig_Teleport_2_Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Dig_Teleport_2_Func001Func001C() ) then
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), "NewDirtEXNofire.mdx")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
        call SetUnitPositionLoc(udg_AlienUnit, GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit()))
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), "NewDirtEXNofire.mdx")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
        call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(udg_AlienPlayer, GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), 0)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Item Ability Removal
//
// 
// NOTE: (Ability being cast) Equal to AbilityArray[(Integer((Name of (Item carried by (Triggering unit) in slot AbilityLoopCount))))]   <---- this is probably wrong, it should be referencing the conversion of a substring. Not the whole string.
// FIX DRILL, IT HAS ISSUES AT 1 CHARGE.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Item_Ability_Removal_Func001Func001Func001Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ItemToRemove != GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 1)) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_ItemToRemove != GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 2)) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_ItemToRemove != GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 3)) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_ItemToRemove != GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 4)) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_ItemToRemove != GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 5)) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_ItemToRemove != GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 6)) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Item_Ability_Removal_Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemCharges(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_AbilityLoopCount)) == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Item_Ability_Removal_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == udg_AbilityArray[S2I(SubStringBJ(GetItemName(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_AbilityLoopCount)), 9, 10))] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Item_Ability_Removal_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_AbilityLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_AbilityLoopCount > 6
        if ( Trig_Item_Ability_Removal_Func001Func001C() ) then
            if ( Trig_Item_Ability_Removal_Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                set udg_ItemToRemove=GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_AbilityLoopCount))
                call RemoveItem(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_AbilityLoopCount))
                if ( Trig_Item_Ability_Removal_Func001Func001Func001Func005C() ) then
                    call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ(GetSpellAbilityId(), GetTriggerUnit())
                else
                    set udg_AbilityLoopCount=6
                endif
            else
                call SetItemCharges(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_AbilityLoopCount), ( GetItemCharges(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_AbilityLoopCount)) - 1 ))
                set udg_AbilityLoopCount=6
            endif
        else
        endif
        set udg_AbilityLoopCount=udg_AbilityLoopCount + 1
    endloop
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Item_Ability_Removal takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Item_Ability_Removal=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Item_Ability_Removal, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Item_Ability_Removal, function Trig_Item_Ability_Removal_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Item Drop
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Item_Drop_Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), udg_AbilityLoopCount)) == GetItemTypeId(GetManipulatedItem()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Item_Drop_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ItemsShared <= 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Item_Drop_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_ItemsShared=0
    set udg_AbilityLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_AbilityLoopCount > 6
        if ( Trig_Item_Drop_Func002Func001C() ) then
            set udg_ItemsShared=( udg_ItemsShared + 1 )
        else
        endif
        set udg_AbilityLoopCount=udg_AbilityLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    if ( Trig_Item_Drop_Func003C() ) then
        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ(udg_AbilityArray[S2I(SubStringBJ(GetItemName(GetManipulatedItem()), 9, 10))], GetManipulatingUnit())
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Item_Drop takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Item_Drop=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Item_Drop, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DROP_ITEM)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Item_Drop, function Trig_Item_Drop_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Grenade
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Grenade_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A01I' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Grenade_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'o003', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "attackground", GetSpellTargetLoc())
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(3.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Grenade takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Grenade=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Grenade, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_CAST)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Grenade, Condition(function Trig_Grenade_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Grenade, function Trig_Grenade_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Gift
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Gift_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetAbilityName(GetSpellAbilityId()), 1, 4) == "Gift" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsPlayerAlly(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( LoadIntegerBJ(0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_VehicleAttackEnabled) != 2 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Gift_Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() == GetSpellTargetUnit() ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Gift_Func001Func001Func004001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h003' )
endfunction

function Trig_Gift_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()) != GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Gift_Func001Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() == GetSpellTargetUnit() ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Gift_Func001Func002Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() == GetSpellTargetUnit() ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Gift_Func001Func002Func002Func004001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h003' )
endfunction

function Trig_Gift_Func001Func002Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()) != GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Gift_Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( ( GetPlayerState(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_FOOD_CAP) - GetPlayerState(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_FOOD_USED) ) >= GetUnitFoodUsed(GetTriggerUnit()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Gift_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) != 'o001' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) != 'o000' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) != 'o002' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) != 'h003' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Gift_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Gift_Func001C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Gift_Func001Func002C() ) then
            if ( Trig_Gift_Func001Func002Func002C() ) then
                call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAllies(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())), ( GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())) + ( " " + ( "has gifted a " + ( GetUnitName(GetTriggerUnit()) + ( " to " + GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())) ) ) ) ) ))
                call SetUnitOwner(GetTriggerUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit()), true)
                if ( (GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h003') ) then // INLINED!!
                    call SetUnitColor(GetTriggerUnit(), PLAYER_COLOR_LIGHT_BLUE)
                else
                    // n
                endif
            else
                if ( Trig_Gift_Func001Func002Func002Func001C() ) then
                    set udg_BuildingToDestroy4Player[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=GetTriggerUnit()
                    call DialogDisplayBJ(true, udg_DestroyBuildingMenu, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
                else
                endif
            endif
        else
            if ( Trig_Gift_Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
                set udg_BuildingToDestroy4Player[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=GetTriggerUnit()
                call DialogDisplayBJ(true, udg_DestroyBuildingMenu, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
            else
                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))], "TRIGSTR_1740")
                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit()))], ( ( GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())) + " tried to gift you a: " ) + ( GetUnitName(GetTriggerUnit()) + " but you do not have enough electricity." ) ))
            endif
        endif
    else
        if ( Trig_Gift_Func001Func001C() ) then
            call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAllies(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())), ( GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())) + ( " " + ( "has gifted a " + ( GetUnitName(GetTriggerUnit()) + ( " to " + GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit())) ) ) ) ) ))
            call SetUnitOwner(GetTriggerUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit()), true)
            if ( (GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h003') ) then // INLINED!!
                call SetUnitColor(GetTriggerUnit(), PLAYER_COLOR_LIGHT_BLUE)
            else
                // n
            endif
        else
            if ( Trig_Gift_Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                set udg_BuildingToDestroy4Player[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=GetTriggerUnit()
                call DialogDisplayBJ(true, udg_DestroyBuildingMenu, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
            else
            endif
        endif
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Gift takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Gift=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Gift, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Gift, Condition(function Trig_Gift_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Gift, function Trig_Gift_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function Trig_Gift_Destroy_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetClickedButtonBJ() == udg_MenuButtons[4] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Gift_Destroy_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call KillUnit(udg_BuildingToDestroy4Player[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())])
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Gift_Destroy=CreateTrigger()

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Marine Death Inheritance
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Marine_Death_Inheritance_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetDyingUnit()) == 'H004' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Marine_Death_Inheritance_Func001Func014Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'h00A' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(GetEnumUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Marine_Death_Inheritance_Func001Func014A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Marine_Death_Inheritance_Func001Func014Func001C() ) then
        call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())), GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit()), 5.00, bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100, 100, 100)
        set udg_RandomInteger=1
    else
        call SetUnitOwner(GetEnumUnit(), Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), true)
        call MakeUnitRescuableToForceBJ(GetEnumUnit(), true, GetPlayersAllies(udg_PlayerToReceiveDatabase))
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Marine_Death_Inheritance_Func001Func016C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_RandomInteger == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( ( udg_HumansGone + udg_HumansDead ) != udg_HumansTotal ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Marine_Death_Inheritance_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitIllusionBJ(GetDyingUnit()) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Marine_Death_Inheritance_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Marine_Death_Inheritance_Func001C() ) then
        call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(udg_AlienUnit, 'I00V'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(udg_AlienUnit, 'I00V')) + 1 ))
        call SetUnitManaBJ(udg_AlienUnit, ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_MANA, udg_AlienUnit) + 1 ))
        set udg_PlayerToReceiveDatabase=GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())
        call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(GetLastCreatedUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()))
        call GroupRemoveUnitSimple(GetDyingUnit(), udg_AllHumansGroup)
        call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), ( GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())) + " did not escape the planet." ))
        set udg_HumansDead=( udg_HumansDead + 1 )
        call ConditionalTriggerExecute(gg_trg_GameEnd_Check)
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > GetPlayerState(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
            call CreateItemLoc('I00L', GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()))
            set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
        endloop
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > GetPlayerState(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER)
            call CreateItemLoc('I00N', GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()))
            set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
        endloop
        call SetPlayerStateBJ(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD, 0)
        call SetPlayerStateBJ(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER, 0)
        set udg_RandomInteger=0
        call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsOfPlayerAll(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())), function Trig_Marine_Death_Inheritance_Func001Func014A)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'H00K', udg_PlayerToReceiveDatabase, GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Database_Zone), bj_UNIT_FACING)
        if ( Trig_Marine_Death_Inheritance_Func001Func016C() ) then
            call DisplayTimedTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(udg_PlayerToReceiveDatabase)], 10.00, "TRIGSTR_2097")
        else
            call DisplayTimedTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(udg_PlayerToReceiveDatabase)], 10.00, "TRIGSTR_2018")
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Marine_Death_Inheritance takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Marine_Death_Inheritance=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Marine_Death_Inheritance, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DEATH)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Marine_Death_Inheritance, Condition(function Trig_Marine_Death_Inheritance_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Marine_Death_Inheritance, function Trig_Marine_Death_Inheritance_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: ScentSeeker Fog
//
// Still needs to look for units with Jug of Sweat
//===========================================================================
function Trig_ScentSeeker_Fog_Func001Func001Func003001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( udg_ScentSeekerLoopCount == 9 )
endfunction

function Trig_ScentSeeker_Fog_Func001Func001Func008001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( udg_ScentSeekerLoopCount == 9 )
endfunction

function Trig_ScentSeeker_Fog_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ScentSeeker == "On" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_ScentSeeker_Fog_Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_ScentSeeker_Fog_Func001Func001C() ) then
        call DestroyEffectBJ(LoadEffectHandleBJ(udg_ScentSeekerLoopCount, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_ScentSeekerHash))
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit()), udg_ScentSeekerPathVar)
        call SaveEffectHandleBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ(), udg_ScentSeekerLoopCount, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_ScentSeekerHash)
        if ( (udg_ScentSeekerLoopCount == 9) ) then // INLINED!!
            set udg_ScentSeekerLoopCount=0
        else
            // n
        endif
    else
        call DestroyEffectBJ(LoadEffectHandleBJ(udg_ScentSeekerLoopCount, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_ScentSeekerHash))
        if ( (udg_ScentSeekerLoopCount == 9) ) then // INLINED!!
            set udg_ScentSeekerLoopCount=0
        else
            // n
        endif
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_ScentSeeker_Fog_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_AllHumansGroup, function Trig_ScentSeeker_Fog_Func001A)
    set udg_ScentSeekerLoopCount=( udg_ScentSeekerLoopCount + 1 )
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_ScentSeeker_Fog takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_ScentSeeker_Fog=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_ScentSeeker_Fog)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_ScentSeeker_Fog, 2)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_ScentSeeker_Fog, function Trig_ScentSeeker_Fog_Actions)
endfunction

        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Picocepa Auto Attack
//
// Shalestorm give multi-Phoenix attack, have attack sound be metal hit.
// Detail Marine Spells, then work on Item spells. Make it add the ability to the marine when an item is received, then make a hotkey per ability and have conditions just check the ability name -1 character so that they still work despite hotkey differences and such.
// Alien Queen: Option only available at start of game. Alien periodically gets lumber to learn new skills. 
// Queen can birth various aliens using mana. She can evolve too and get abilities that recouperate mana more quickly.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Picocepa_Auto_Attack_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetOrderTargetUnit()) == 'n001' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitCurrentOrder(GetTriggerUnit()) == String2OrderIdBJ("smart") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerController(GetOwningPlayer(udg_HydraUnit)) != MAP_CONTROL_USER ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Picocepa_Auto_Attack_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), "attack", GetOrderTargetUnit())
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Picocepa_Auto_Attack takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Picocepa_Auto_Attack=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Picocepa_Auto_Attack, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ISSUED_TARGET_ORDER)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Picocepa_Auto_Attack, Condition(function Trig_Picocepa_Auto_Attack_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Picocepa_Auto_Attack, function Trig_Picocepa_Auto_Attack_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Szethik Isturi
//
// Shalestorm give multi-Phoenix attack, have attack sound be metal hit.
// Detail Marine Spells, then work on Item spells. Make it add the ability to the marine when an item is received, then make a hotkey per ability and have conditions just check the ability name -1 character so that they still work despite hotkey differences and such.
// Alien Queen: Option only available at start of game. Alien periodically gets lumber to learn new skills. 
// Queen can birth various aliens using mana. She can evolve too and get abilities that recouperate mana more quickly.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Szethik_Isturi_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetOrderTargetUnit()) == 'n005' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitCurrentOrder(GetTriggerUnit()) == String2OrderIdBJ("smart") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerController(GetOwningPlayer(udg_HydraUnit)) != MAP_CONTROL_USER ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Szethik_Isturi_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), "attack", GetOrderTargetUnit())
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Szethik_Isturi takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Szethik_Isturi=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Szethik_Isturi, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ISSUED_TARGET_ORDER)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Szethik_Isturi, Condition(function Trig_Szethik_Isturi_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Szethik_Isturi, function Trig_Szethik_Isturi_Actions)
endfunction

// Trigger: Rocket Auto Attack
//
// Shalestorm give multi-Phoenix attack, have attack sound be metal hit.
// Detail Marine Spells, then work on Item spells. Make it add the ability to the marine when an item is received, then make a hotkey per ability and have conditions just check the ability name -1 character so that they still work despite hotkey differences and such.
// Alien Queen: Option only available at start of game. Alien periodically gets lumber to learn new skills. 
// Queen can birth various aliens using mana. She can evolve too and get abilities that recouperate mana more quickly.

        return false
    endif

        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetOrderedUnit() == udg_AlienUnit ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Listen To Fear
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func002001003 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( 'H004' == GetUnitTypeId(GetFilterUnit()) )
endfunction

function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(GetEnumUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func002A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func002Func001C() ) then
        call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetEnumUnit(), udg_HeartBeatRangeGroup)
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func003Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit()), GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit)) < DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_HeartBeatChosenUnit), GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit)) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func003Func002A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func003Func002Func001C() ) then
        set udg_HeartBeatChosenUnit=GetEnumUnit()
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func003Func003Func005001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_HeartBeatChosenUnit), GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit)) <= 2500.00 )
endfunction

function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func003Func003Func006001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_HeartBeatChosenUnit), GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit)) <= 1400.00 )
endfunction

function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func003Func003Func007001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_HeartBeatChosenUnit), GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit)) <= 850.00 )
endfunction

function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func003Func003Func009C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_HeartBeatFrequency >= udg_HeartBeatThreshold ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func003Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( CountUnitsInGroup(udg_HeartBeatRangeGroup) >= 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( CountUnitsInGroup(udg_HeartBeatRangeGroup) >= 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsInRangeOfLocMatching(3000.00, GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), Condition(function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func002001003)), function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func002A)
    if ( Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func003C() ) then
        set udg_HeartBeatChosenUnit=GroupPickRandomUnit(udg_HeartBeatRangeGroup)
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_HeartBeatRangeGroup, function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func003Func002A)
        if ( Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func003Func003C() ) then
            set udg_HeartBeatThreshold=2.50
            set udg_HeartBeatFrequency=( udg_HeartBeatFrequency + 0.50 )
            set udg_HeartBeatDistancePercent=( 100.00 - ( 0.03 * DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), GetUnitLoc(udg_HeartBeatChosenUnit)) ) )
            if ( (DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_HeartBeatChosenUnit), GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit)) <= 2500.00) ) then // INLINED!!
                set udg_HeartBeatThreshold=2.00
            else
                // n
            endif
            if ( (DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_HeartBeatChosenUnit), GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit)) <= 1400.00) ) then // INLINED!!
                set udg_HeartBeatThreshold=1.50
            else
                // n
            endif
            if ( (DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_HeartBeatChosenUnit), GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit)) <= 850.00) ) then // INLINED!!
                set udg_HeartBeatThreshold=1.00
            else
                // n
            endif
            call GroupRemoveGroup(udg_HeartBeatRangeGroup, udg_HeartBeatRangeGroup)
            if ( Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Func003Func003Func009C() ) then
                call SetSoundPitchBJ(gg_snd_HeartBeat, RMaxBJ(0.75, ( 1.04 * ( 0.01 * udg_HeartBeatDistancePercent ) )))
                call PlaySoundFromOffsetBJ(udg_HeartBeatVariable, RMaxBJ(20.00, udg_HeartBeatDistancePercent), 0)
                call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_AlienTeam, GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), ( udg_HeartBeatThreshold / 2.00 ), bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, ( udg_HeartBeatDistancePercent + 10.00 ), 0.00, 0.00)
                set udg_HeartBeatFrequency=0.00
            else
            endif
        else
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Listen_To_Fear takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Listen_To_Fear=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Listen_To_Fear)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Listen_To_Fear, 0.50)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Listen_To_Fear, function Trig_Listen_To_Fear_Actions)
endfunction

endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: GameEnd Check
//===========================================================================
function Trig_GameEnd_Check_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( ( udg_HumansGone + udg_HumansDead ) == udg_HumansTotal ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_GameEnd_Check_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_1666")
    call TriggerSleepAction(5.00)
    call DialogSetMessageBJ(udg_EndGameStatsMenu, ( udg_zHumansLost + ( "|n|n" + ( udg_zHumansSaved + ( "|n|n" + udg_zAlienStatus ) ) ) ))
    call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_EndGameStatsMenu, "TRIGSTR_2208")
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > 12
        call DialogDisplayBJ(true, udg_EndGameStatsMenu, ConvertedPlayer(udg_GenericLoopCount))
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Humans_Lost_Reveal)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_GameEnd_Check takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_GameEnd_Check=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_GameEnd_Check)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_GameEnd_Check, Condition(function Trig_GameEnd_Check_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_GameEnd_Check, function Trig_GameEnd_Check_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Humans Lost Reveal
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Humans_Lost_Reveal_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_zRandomStatsFlairCount == 45 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Humans_Lost_Reveal_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_zHumansLost=( "Humans Lost: " + I2S(GetRandomInt(10000, 99999)) )
    call DialogSetMessageBJ(udg_EndGameStatsMenu, ( udg_zHumansLost + ( "|n|n" + ( udg_zHumansSaved + ( "|n|n" + udg_zAlienStatus ) ) ) ))
    set udg_zRandomStatsFlairCount=( udg_zRandomStatsFlairCount + 1 )
    if ( Trig_Humans_Lost_Reveal_Func005C() ) then
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
        set udg_zRandomStatsFlairCount=0
        set udg_zHumansLost=( "Humans Lost: " + ( "|c00FF0000" + ( I2S(udg_HumansDead) + "|r" ) ) )
        call DialogSetMessageBJ(udg_EndGameStatsMenu, ( udg_zHumansLost + ( "|n|n" + ( udg_zHumansSaved + ( "|n|n" + udg_zAlienStatus ) ) ) ))
        call TriggerSleepAction(1.50)
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Humans_Saved_Reveal)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Humans_Lost_Reveal takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Humans_Lost_Reveal=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Humans_Lost_Reveal)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Humans_Lost_Reveal, 0.05)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Humans_Lost_Reveal, function Trig_Humans_Lost_Reveal_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Humans Saved Reveal
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Humans_Saved_Reveal_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_zRandomStatsFlairCount == 45 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Humans_Saved_Reveal_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_zHumansSaved=( "Humans Saved: " + I2S(GetRandomInt(10000, 99999)) )
    call DialogSetMessageBJ(udg_EndGameStatsMenu, ( udg_zHumansLost + ( "|n|n" + ( udg_zHumansSaved + ( "|n|n" + udg_zAlienStatus ) ) ) ))
    set udg_zRandomStatsFlairCount=( udg_zRandomStatsFlairCount + 1 )
    if ( Trig_Humans_Saved_Reveal_Func005C() ) then
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
        set udg_zRandomStatsFlairCount=0
        set udg_zHumansSaved=( "Humans Saved: " + ( "|c0096FF96" + ( I2S(( udg_HumansTotal - udg_HumansDead )) + "|r" ) ) )
        call DialogSetMessageBJ(udg_EndGameStatsMenu, ( udg_zHumansLost + ( "|n|n" + ( udg_zHumansSaved + ( "|n|n" + udg_zAlienStatus ) ) ) ))
        call TriggerSleepAction(1.50)
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Alien_Status)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Humans_Saved_Reveal takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Humans_Saved_Reveal=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Humans_Saved_Reveal)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Humans_Saved_Reveal, 0.05)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Humans_Saved_Reveal, function Trig_Humans_Saved_Reveal_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Alien Status
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Alien_Status_Func009Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(udg_AlienUnit) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Alien_Status_Func009C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_zRandomStatsFlairCount == 45 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Alien_Status_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_zRandomLetterGenerator[1]=GetRandomInt(1, 26)
    set udg_zRandomLetterGenerator[2]=GetRandomInt(1, 26)
    set udg_zRandomLetterGenerator[3]=GetRandomInt(1, 26)
    set udg_zRandomLetterGenerator[4]=GetRandomInt(1, 26)
    set udg_zAlienStatus=( "Alien Status: " + ( SubStringBJ(udg_zRandomLetterPath, udg_zRandomLetterGenerator[1], udg_zRandomLetterGenerator[1]) + ( SubStringBJ(udg_zRandomLetterPath, udg_zRandomLetterGenerator[2], udg_zRandomLetterGenerator[2]) + ( SubStringBJ(udg_zRandomLetterPath, udg_zRandomLetterGenerator[3], udg_zRandomLetterGenerator[3]) + SubStringBJ(udg_zRandomLetterPath, udg_zRandomLetterGenerator[4], udg_zRandomLetterGenerator[4]) ) ) ) )
    call DialogSetMessageBJ(udg_EndGameStatsMenu, ( udg_zHumansLost + ( "|n|n" + ( udg_zHumansSaved + ( "|n|n" + udg_zAlienStatus ) ) ) ))
    set udg_zRandomStatsFlairCount=( udg_zRandomStatsFlairCount + 1 )
    if ( Trig_Alien_Status_Func009C() ) then
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
        set udg_zRandomStatsFlairCount=0
        if ( Trig_Alien_Status_Func009Func003C() ) then
            set udg_zAlienStatus=( "Alien Status: " + ( "|c00FF7F00" + ( "Alive|r" ) ) )
        else
            set udg_zAlienStatus=( "Alien Status: " + ( "|c00FF7F00Dead" ) )
        endif
        call DialogSetMessageBJ(udg_EndGameStatsMenu, ( udg_zHumansLost + ( "|n|n" + ( udg_zHumansSaved + ( "|n|n" + udg_zAlienStatus ) ) ) ))
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Alien_Status takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Alien_Status=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Alien_Status)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Alien_Status, 0.05)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Alien_Status, function Trig_Alien_Status_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Add Tutorial
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Add_Tutorial_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTriggerPlayer() == udg_AlienPlayer ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Add_Tutorial_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())], "TRIGSTR_2221")
    if ( Trig_Add_Tutorial_Func002C() ) then
        call ForceAddPlayerSimple(GetTriggerPlayer(), udg_TutorialPlayersAlien)
    else
        call ForceAddPlayerSimple(GetTriggerPlayer(), udg_TutorialPlayersHuman)
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Add_Tutorial takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Add_Tutorial=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Add_Tutorial, Player(0), "-new", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Add_Tutorial, Player(1), "-new", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Add_Tutorial, Player(2), "-new", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Add_Tutorial, Player(3), "-new", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Add_Tutorial, Player(4), "-new", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Add_Tutorial, Player(5), "-new", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Add_Tutorial, Player(6), "-new", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Add_Tutorial, Player(7), "-new", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Add_Tutorial, Player(8), "-new", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Add_Tutorial, Player(9), "-new", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Add_Tutorial, Player(10), "-new", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Add_Tutorial, Player(11), "-new", true)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Add_Tutorial, function Trig_Add_Tutorial_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================

    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetDyingUnit()) == 'e001' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

    call RemoveUnit(GetDyingUnit())
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Darklight_Dies=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Darklight_Dies, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DEATH)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Darklight_Dies, Condition(function Trig_Darklight_Dies_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Darklight_Dies, function Trig_Darklight_Dies_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Darklight Teleport
//
// Make a special effect for the actual teleport
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Darklight_Teleport_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetAbilityName(GetSpellAbilityId()), 1, 19) == "Teleport: Darklight" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Darklight_Teleport_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(udg_ActiveDarklight) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Darklight_Teleport_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTerrainPathableBJ(GetUnitLoc(udg_ActiveDarklight), PATHING_TYPE_WALKABILITY) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Darklight_Teleport_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Darklight_Teleport_Func001C() ) then
        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, "TRIGSTR_1775")
        call IssueImmediateOrderBJ(udg_AlienUnit, "stop")
        set udg_DarklightAnimationStepCounter=0
        return
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Darklight_Teleport_Func004C() ) then
        call IssueImmediateOrderBJ(udg_AlienUnit, "stop")
        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, "TRIGSTR_1711")
    else
        call PauseUnitBJ(true, udg_ActiveDarklight)
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Darklight_Shrink_1)
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Darklight_Teleport takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Darklight_Teleport=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Darklight_Teleport, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_CAST)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Darklight_Teleport, Condition(function Trig_Darklight_Teleport_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Darklight_Teleport, function Trig_Darklight_Teleport_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Darklight Shrink 1
//
// currently able to teleport to zones alien shouldn't go. Check walkability
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Darklight_Shrink_1_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(udg_ActiveDarklight) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Darklight_Shrink_1_Func006C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_DarklightAnimationStepCounter == 50 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Darklight_Shrink_1_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Darklight_Shrink_1_Func001C() ) then
        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, "TRIGSTR_1776")
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
        set udg_DarklightAnimationStepCounter=0
        return
    else
    endif
    set udg_DarklightAnimationStepCounter=( udg_DarklightAnimationStepCounter + 1 )
    set udg_DarklightSizeAmount=( udg_DarklightSizeAmount - 1 )
    call SetUnitFlyHeightBJ(udg_ActiveDarklight, 120.00, 240.00)
    call SetUnitScalePercent(udg_ActiveDarklight, udg_DarklightSizeAmount, udg_DarklightSizeAmount, udg_DarklightSizeAmount)
    if ( Trig_Darklight_Shrink_1_Func006C() ) then
        set udg_DarklightAnimationStepCounter=0
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Darklight_Grow_2)
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Darklight_Shrink_1 takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Darklight_Shrink_1=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Darklight_Shrink_1)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Darklight_Shrink_1, 0.01)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Darklight_Shrink_1, function Trig_Darklight_Shrink_1_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Darklight Up GrowFastCrash 9
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Darklight_Up_GrowFastCrash_9_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(udg_ActiveDarklight) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Darklight_Up_GrowFastCrash_9_Func007C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_DarklightAnimationStepCounter == 75 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Darklight_Up_GrowFastCrash_9_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Darklight_Up_GrowFastCrash_9_Func001C() ) then
        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, "TRIGSTR_1784")
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
        set udg_DarklightAnimationStepCounter=0
        return
    else
    endif
    call SetUnitFlyHeightBJ(udg_ActiveDarklight, 0.00, 540.00)
    set udg_DarklightAnimationStepCounter=( udg_DarklightAnimationStepCounter + 1 )
    set udg_DarklightSizeAmount=( udg_DarklightSizeAmount + 2.00 )
    call SetUnitTimeScalePercent(udg_ActiveDarklight, ( udg_DarklightSizeAmount * 2.00 ))
    call SetUnitScalePercent(udg_ActiveDarklight, udg_DarklightSizeAmount, udg_DarklightSizeAmount, udg_DarklightSizeAmount)
    if ( Trig_Darklight_Up_GrowFastCrash_9_Func007C() ) then
        set udg_DarklightAnimationStepCounter=0
        set udg_DarklightSizeAmount=100.00
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), "DarkWarp.mdx")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
        call SetUnitPositionLoc(udg_AlienUnit, GetUnitLoc(udg_ActiveDarklight))
        call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(udg_AlienPlayer, GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), 0)
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), "DarkWarp.mdx")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
        call RemoveUnit(udg_ActiveDarklight)
        call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(udg_AlienUnit, udg_AlienPlayer)
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Darklight_Up_GrowFastCrash_9 takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Darklight_Up_GrowFastCrash_9=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Darklight_Up_GrowFastCrash_9)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Darklight_Up_GrowFastCrash_9, 0.01)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Darklight_Up_GrowFastCrash_9, function Trig_Darklight_Up_GrowFastCrash_9_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Reform Darklight
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Reform_Darklight_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A05B' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Reform_Darklight_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Autowander)
    call RemoveUnit(udg_ActiveDarklight)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'e001', udg_AlienPlayer, GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_ActiveDarklight=GetLastCreatedUnit()
    call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(udg_AlienPlayer, GetUnitLoc(udg_ActiveDarklight), 0)
    call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(udg_ActiveDarklight, udg_AlienPlayer)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Reform_Darklight takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Reform_Darklight=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Reform_Darklight)
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Reform_Darklight, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Reform_Darklight, Condition(function Trig_Reform_Darklight_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Reform_Darklight, function Trig_Reform_Darklight_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Darklight Found Victim
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Darklight_Found_Victim_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(udg_ActiveDarklight) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_MANA, udg_ActiveDarklight) >= 99.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Darklight_Found_Victim_Func004Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_ActiveDarklight), GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())) <= 700.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Darklight_Found_Victim_Func004A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Darklight_Found_Victim_Func004Func001C() ) then
        set udg_DarkLightLocate=1
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Darklight_Found_Victim_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_DarkLightLocate == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Darklight_Found_Victim_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_DarkLightLocate=0
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_AllHumansGroup, function Trig_Darklight_Found_Victim_Func004A)
    if ( Trig_Darklight_Found_Victim_Func005C() ) then
        call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_AlienTeam, GetUnitLoc(udg_ActiveDarklight), 2.00, bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100, 100, 100)
        call PlaySoundBJ(udg_DarklightSound)
        call SetUnitManaBJ(udg_ActiveDarklight, 0)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Darklight_Found_Victim takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Darklight_Found_Victim=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Darklight_Found_Victim)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Darklight_Found_Victim, 2)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Darklight_Found_Victim, Condition(function Trig_Darklight_Found_Victim_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Darklight_Found_Victim, function Trig_Darklight_Found_Victim_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Autowander
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Autowander_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitCurrentOrder(udg_ActiveDarklight) == String2OrderIdBJ("") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Autowander_Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTerrainPathableBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, PATHING_TYPE_FLYABILITY) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Autowander_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
    set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > 2
        if ( Trig_Autowander_Func002Func001C() ) then
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
            set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
        else
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=2
            call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(udg_ActiveDarklight, "move", udg_RandomPositionTarget)
        endif
        set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
    endloop
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Autowander takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Autowander=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Autowander)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Autowander, 4.00)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Autowander, Condition(function Trig_Autowander_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Autowander, function Trig_Autowander_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: AutoWander Toggle
//===========================================================================
function Trig_AutoWander_Toggle_Func003001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetIssuedOrderIdBJ() == String2OrderIdBJ("immolation") )
endfunction

function Trig_AutoWander_Toggle_Func003002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetIssuedOrderIdBJ() == String2OrderIdBJ("unimmolation") )
endfunction

function Trig_AutoWander_Toggle_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'e001' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not GetBooleanOr((GetIssuedOrderIdBJ() == String2OrderIdBJ("immolation")), (GetIssuedOrderIdBJ() == String2OrderIdBJ("unimmolation"))) ) then // INLINED!!
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_AutoWander_Toggle_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTriggerEnabled(gg_trg_Autowander) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_AutoWander_Toggle_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_AutoWander_Toggle_Func001C() ) then
        call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Autowander)
        call IssueImmediateOrderBJ(udg_ActiveDarklight, "stop")
    else
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Autowander)
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_AutoWander_Toggle takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_AutoWander_Toggle=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_AutoWander_Toggle)
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_AutoWander_Toggle, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ISSUED_ORDER)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_AutoWander_Toggle, Condition(function Trig_AutoWander_Toggle_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_AutoWander_Toggle, function Trig_AutoWander_Toggle_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function Trig_Tank_Creation_AddGroup_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'o002' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Tank_Creation_AddGroup_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'o000' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Tank_Creation_AddGroup_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'o001' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Tank_Creation_AddGroup_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Tank_Creation_AddGroup_Func001C() ) then
        call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetTrainedUnit(), udg_StormFrontTanksGroup)
        call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetTrainedUnit(), udg_TotalTanksGroup)
        call SetUnitColor(GetTrainedUnit(), PLAYER_COLOR_MAROON)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Tank_Creation_AddGroup_Func002C() ) then
        call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetTrainedUnit(), udg_ReconTanksGroup)
        call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetTrainedUnit(), udg_TotalTanksGroup)
        call SetUnitColor(GetTrainedUnit(), PLAYER_COLOR_MAROON)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Tank_Creation_AddGroup_Func003C() ) then
        call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetTrainedUnit(), udg_ApocalypseTankGroup)
        call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetTrainedUnit(), udg_TotalTanksGroup)
        call SetUnitColor(GetTrainedUnit(), PLAYER_COLOR_MAROON)
    else
    endif
endfunction

    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Tank_Creation_AddGroup, function Trig_Tank_Creation_AddGroup_Actions)

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Carrying Rocket Check
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Carrying_Rocket_Check_Func001Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitInTransportBJ(udg_TotalRockets[udg_GenericLoopCount], GetEnumUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Carrying_Rocket_Check_Func001Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_GenericSubLoopCount == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Carrying_Rocket_Check_Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=0
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > udg_TotalRocketInt
        if ( Trig_Carrying_Rocket_Check_Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
        else
        endif
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    if ( Trig_Carrying_Rocket_Check_Func001Func003C() ) then
        call IssueTargetOrderBJ(udg_RocketBuffer, "innerfire", GetEnumUnit())
    else
        call UnitRemoveBuffBJ('B002', GetEnumUnit())
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Carrying_Rocket_Check_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TotalTanksGroup, function Trig_Carrying_Rocket_Check_Func001A)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Carrying_Rocket_Check takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Carrying_Rocket_Check=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Carrying_Rocket_Check, 0.50)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Carrying_Rocket_Check, function Trig_Carrying_Rocket_Check_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Tank Death
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Tank_Death_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitInGroup(GetDyingUnit(), udg_TotalTanksGroup) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Tank_Death_Func002Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetEnumUnit() == udg_PlayerUnitMatch[udg_xSpawnNumberLoop] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Tank_Death_Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'H004' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() != udg_PlayerUnitMatch[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitIllusionBJ(GetTriggerUnit()) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Tank_Death_Func002A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Tank_Death_Func002Func001C() ) then
        set udg_xSpawnNumberLoop=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_xSpawnNumberLoop > 12
            if ( Trig_Tank_Death_Func002Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                set udg_UnitPlayerIteration=udg_xSpawnNumberLoop
                set udg_xSpawnNumberLoop=12
            else
            endif
            set udg_xSpawnNumberLoop=udg_xSpawnNumberLoop + 1
        endloop
        call SetUnitOwner(GetEnumUnit(), ConvertedPlayer(udg_UnitPlayerIteration), true)
        call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(GetEnumUnit(), ConvertedPlayer(udg_UnitPlayerIteration))
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Tank_Death_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call GroupRemoveUnitSimple(GetDyingUnit(), udg_TotalTanksGroup)
    call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(512, GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())), function Trig_Tank_Death_Func002A)
endfunction

function InitTrig_Tank_Death takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Tank_Death=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Tank_Death, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DEATH)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Tank_Death, Condition(function Trig_Tank_Death_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Tank_Death, function Trig_Tank_Death_Actions)
endfunction

        return false

    return true
endfunction

    if ( Trig_Temporal_Flux_Func004Func001C() ) then

    else
    endif
endfunction

    call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsInRangeOfLocMatching(800.00, GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), Condition(function Trig_Temporal_Flux_Func004001003)), function Trig_Temporal_Flux_Func004A)
    call RemoveUnit(GetLastCreatedUnit())

    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A00N' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Nanite_Repair_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetTriggerUnit()) != GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_MAX_LIFE, GetTriggerUnit()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Nanite_Repair_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Nanite_Repair_Func001C() ) then
        call SetUnitLifeBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetTriggerUnit()) + 100.00 ))
    else
        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))], "TRIGSTR_299")
        call SetPlayerStateBJ(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD, ( GetPlayerState(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD) + 1 ))
    endif
endfunction

// Trigger: Tank Enter
//
// Make a Bind to tank option for rocket?
// Make another trigger that runs or alter this one so that when a rocket enters a transport it saves that transport into a group, then periodically check the group members to see if a rocket is in them or something.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Tank_Enter_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTransportUnitBJ()) != 'u003' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetLoadedUnitBJ()) != 'h00E' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true

    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Tank_Enter, function Trig_Tank_Enter_Actions)

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Stormfront Pilot Check
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Stormfront_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001Func001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()) != 0.01 )
endfunction

function Trig_Stormfront_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001Func003001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()) == 0.01 )
endfunction

function Trig_Stormfront_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001Func007Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitInTransportBJ(LoadUnitHandleBJ(udg_AbilityLoopCount, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleHash), GetEnumUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Stormfront_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit()) != 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Stormfront_Pilot_Check_Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Stormfront_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001C() ) then
        if ( (GetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()) == 0.01) ) then // INLINED!!
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A03T', GetEnumUnit())
        else
            call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A02D', GetEnumUnit())
        endif
        call SaveIntegerBJ(2, 0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleAttackEnabled)
        call SetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit(), GetUnitDefaultMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()))
        set udg_AbilityLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_AbilityLoopCount > GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit())
            if ( Trig_Stormfront_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001Func007Func001C() ) then
            else
                call SaveUnitHandleBJ(LoadUnitHandleBJ(udg_AbilityLoopCount, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleHash), GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit()), GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleHash)
                call SetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit()) - 1 ))
                set udg_AbilityLoopCount=( udg_AbilityLoopCount - 1 )
            endif
            set udg_AbilityLoopCount=udg_AbilityLoopCount + 1
        endloop
    else
        if ( (GetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()) != 0.01) ) then // INLINED!!
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A02D', GetEnumUnit())
        else
            call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A02D', GetEnumUnit())
        endif
        call SaveIntegerBJ(1, 0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleAttackEnabled)
        call SetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit(), 0.01)
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Stormfront_Pilot_Check_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_StormFrontTanksGroup, function Trig_Stormfront_Pilot_Check_Func001A)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Stormfront_Pilot_Check takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Stormfront_Pilot_Check=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Stormfront_Pilot_Check, 0.50)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Stormfront_Pilot_Check, function Trig_Stormfront_Pilot_Check_Actions)
endfunction

//
// Maybe make a tank mount ability on the rocket.
