    return ( GetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()) == 0.01 )
endfunction

function Trig_Recon_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001Func007Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitInTransportBJ(LoadUnitHandleBJ(udg_AbilityLoopCount, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleHash), GetEnumUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Recon_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit()) != 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Recon_Pilot_Check_Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Recon_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001C() ) then
        if ( (GetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()) == 0.01) ) then // INLINED!!
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A03T', GetEnumUnit())
        else
            call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A02D', GetEnumUnit())
        endif
        call SaveIntegerBJ(2, 0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleAttackEnabled)
        call SetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit(), GetUnitDefaultMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()))
        set udg_AbilityLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_AbilityLoopCount > GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit())
            if ( Trig_Recon_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001Func007Func001C() ) then
            else
                call SaveUnitHandleBJ(LoadUnitHandleBJ(udg_AbilityLoopCount, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleHash), GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit()), GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleHash)
                call SetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit()) - 1 ))
                set udg_AbilityLoopCount=( udg_AbilityLoopCount - 1 )
            endif
            set udg_AbilityLoopCount=udg_AbilityLoopCount + 1
        endloop
    else
        if ( (GetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()) != 0.01) ) then // INLINED!!
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A02D', GetEnumUnit())
        else
            call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A02D', GetEnumUnit())
        endif
        call SaveIntegerBJ(1, 0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleAttackEnabled)
        call SetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit(), 0.01)
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Recon_Pilot_Check_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_ReconTanksGroup, function Trig_Recon_Pilot_Check_Func001A)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Recon_Pilot_Check takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Recon_Pilot_Check=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Recon_Pilot_Check, 0.50)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Recon_Pilot_Check, function Trig_Recon_Pilot_Check_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Apocalypse Pilot Check
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001Func001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()) != 0.01 )
endfunction

function Trig_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001Func003001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()) == 0.01 )
endfunction

function Trig_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001Func007Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitInTransportBJ(LoadUnitHandleBJ(udg_AbilityLoopCount, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleHash), GetEnumUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit()) != 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check_Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001C() ) then
        if ( (GetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()) == 0.01) ) then // INLINED!!
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A03T', GetEnumUnit())
        else
            call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A02D', GetEnumUnit())
        endif
        call SaveIntegerBJ(2, 0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleAttackEnabled)
        call SetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit(), GetUnitDefaultMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()))
        set udg_AbilityLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_AbilityLoopCount > GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit())
            if ( Trig_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check_Func001Func001Func007Func001C() ) then
            else
                call SaveUnitHandleBJ(LoadUnitHandleBJ(udg_AbilityLoopCount, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleHash), GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit()), GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleHash)
                call SetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit()) - 1 ))
                set udg_AbilityLoopCount=( udg_AbilityLoopCount - 1 )
            endif
            set udg_AbilityLoopCount=udg_AbilityLoopCount + 1
        endloop
    else
        if ( (GetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit()) != 0.01) ) then // INLINED!!
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A02D', GetEnumUnit())
        else
            call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A02D', GetEnumUnit())
        endif
        call SaveIntegerBJ(1, 0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetEnumUnit()), udg_VehicleAttackEnabled)
        call SetUnitMoveSpeed(GetEnumUnit(), 0.01)
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_ApocalypseTankGroup, function Trig_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check_Func001A)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check, 0.50)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check, function Trig_Apocalypse_Pilot_Check_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Rocket ForceBoard
//
// Make it so when a unit clicks rocket if its a human it gives rocket to that human then back to its other owner.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Rocket_ForceBoard_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'H004' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetOrderTargetUnit()) == 'h00F' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitCurrentOrder(GetTriggerUnit()) == String2OrderIdBJ("smart") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Rocket_ForceBoard_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), GetUnitLoc(GetOrderTargetUnit())) <= 235.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Rocket_ForceBoard_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Rocket_ForceBoard_Func005C() ) then
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
        set udg_BoardingHuman=GetTriggerUnit()
        set udg_BoardingRocket=GetOrderTargetUnit()
        set udg_BoardingHumanOwner=GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())
        set udg_RocketOwner=GetOwningPlayer(GetOrderTargetUnit())
        call SetUnitOwner(udg_BoardingRocket, udg_BoardingHumanOwner, false)
        call IssueTargetOrderBJ(udg_BoardingRocket, "load", udg_BoardingHuman)
        call TriggerSleepAction(0.00)
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Rocket_ForceBoard)
        call SetUnitOwner(udg_BoardingRocket, udg_RocketOwner, false)
        call SetUnitOwner(udg_BoardingHuman, udg_BoardingHumanOwner, false)
    else
        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetOrderedUnit()))], "TRIGSTR_2095")
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Rocket_ForceBoard takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Rocket_ForceBoard=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Rocket_ForceBoard, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ISSUED_TARGET_ORDER)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Rocket_ForceBoard, Condition(function Trig_Rocket_ForceBoard_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Rocket_ForceBoard, function Trig_Rocket_ForceBoard_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Mount the Rocket
//
// ALL CARGO MADE 1:1
// instead of 2:1. See if it broke anything, like tanks?
// Make Rocket an Enemy to AlienPlayer
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Mount_the_Rocket_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A043' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSpellTargetUnit()) == 'h00E' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Mount_the_Rocket_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetUnitManaBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetSpellTargetUnit()))
    call RemoveUnit(GetSpellTargetUnit())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'h00F', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call SetUnitPathing(GetLastCreatedUnit(), false)
    call SetUnitColor(GetLastCreatedUnit(), PLAYER_COLOR_CYAN)
    call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("overhead", GetLastCreatedUnit(), "RocketPower.mdx")
    call SaveUnitHandleBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), 0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_RocketPairingHash)
    call SetUnitPositionLoc(GetLastCreatedUnit(), OffsetLocation(GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), 15.00, 20.00))
    call SetUnitLifeBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_MANA, GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetUnitInvulnerable(GetTriggerUnit(), true)
    call SetUnitManaBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 0)
    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A045', GetTriggerUnit())
    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A046', GetTriggerUnit())
    call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A043', GetTriggerUnit())
    call IssueImmediateOrderBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), "immolation")
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Mount_the_Rocket takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Mount_the_Rocket=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Mount_the_Rocket, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_CAST)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Mount_the_Rocket, Condition(function Trig_Mount_the_Rocket_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Mount_the_Rocket, function Trig_Mount_the_Rocket_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Liftoff
//
// ALL CARGO MADE 1:1
// instead of 2:1. See if it broke anything, like tanks?
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Liftoff_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A046' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Liftoff_Func016Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( LoadStringBJ(udg_GenericLoopCount, GetHandleIdBJ(udg_RocketReference), udg_VictoryHash) != "" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Liftoff_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(udg_RocketBlinderCaster, "silence", GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetUnitInvulnerable(GetTriggerUnit(), false)
    call SetUnitLifeBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetTriggerUnit()) - 2000.00 ))
    call SetUnitManaBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 0)
    call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A045', GetTriggerUnit())
    call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A046', GetTriggerUnit())
    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A043', GetTriggerUnit())
    call SetUnitMoveSpeed(LoadUnitHandleBJ(0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_RocketPairingHash), 1.00)
    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('Arav', LoadUnitHandleBJ(0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_RocketPairingHash))
    call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('Arav', LoadUnitHandleBJ(0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_RocketPairingHash))
    call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", LoadUnitHandleBJ(0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_RocketPairingHash), "RocketLaunchEffect.mdx")
    call SetUnitFlyHeightBJ(LoadUnitHandleBJ(0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_RocketPairingHash), 12000.00, 375.00)
    call SetUnitInvulnerable(LoadUnitHandleBJ(0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_RocketPairingHash), true)
    set udg_RocketReference=LoadUnitHandleBJ(0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_RocketPairingHash)
    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_1216")
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > 8
        if ( Trig_Liftoff_Func016Func001C() ) then
            call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), ( LoadStringBJ(udg_GenericLoopCount, GetHandleIdBJ(udg_RocketReference), udg_VictoryHash) + " has achieved victory!" ))
            set udg_HumansGone=( udg_HumansGone + 1 )
        else
        endif
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    call GroupAddUnitSimple(LoadUnitHandleBJ(0, GetHandleIdBJ(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_RocketPairingHash), udg_RocketsToBeMoved)
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Rocket_Removal)
    call ConditionalTriggerExecute(gg_trg_GameEnd_Check)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Liftoff takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Liftoff=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Liftoff, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_FINISH)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Liftoff, Condition(function Trig_Liftoff_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Liftoff, function Trig_Liftoff_Actions)
endfunction

//
// ALL CARGO MADE 1:1
// instead of 2:1. See if it broke anything, like tanks?
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Rocket_Removal_Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit()) == 4 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Rocket_Removal_Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitUserData(GetEnumUnit()) + 1 ))
    if ( Trig_Rocket_Removal_Func001Func002C() ) then
        call SetUnitPositionLoc(GetEnumUnit(), GetRectCenter(gg_rct_RocketHoldRegion))
        call GroupRemoveUnitSimple(GetEnumUnit(), udg_RocketsToBeMoved)
    else
    endif
endfunction

        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

    call ForGroupBJ(udg_RocketsToBeMoved, function Trig_Rocket_Removal_Func001A)
    if ( Trig_Rocket_Removal_Func002C() ) then
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
    else
    endif
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Rocket_Removal=CreateTrigger()

    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Rocket_Removal, function Trig_Rocket_Removal_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Ignition
//
// ALL CARGO MADE 1:1
// instead of 2:1. See if it broke anything, like tanks?
// Make a variable for RocketSoundtrack so that it cant overlap, silence it if another rocket fires.
// Make the 4 soundtracks into an array. Then loop the array checking that the same number isn't chosen twice. if it is reloop it.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Ignition_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A046' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ignition_Func006Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_LastPlayedSound == udg_RandomInteger ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ignition_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call PlaySoundBJ(gg_snd_Rocket)
    call StopSoundBJ(udg_RocketSoundtrack, true)
    call PingMinimapLocForForce(GetPlayersAll(), GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), 10.00)
    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_1235")
    set udg_RandomInteger=GetRandomInt(1, 4)
    set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > 2
        if ( Trig_Ignition_Func006Func001C() ) then
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
            set udg_RandomInteger=GetRandomInt(1, 4)
        else
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=2
            set udg_LastPlayedSound=udg_RandomInteger
        endif
        set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    call PlaySoundBJ(udg_RocketSoundVariation[udg_RandomInteger])
    set udg_RocketSoundtrack=GetLastPlayedSound()
    call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_RocketFuelRestoreGroup)
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_RocketFuelRestore)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Ignition takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Ignition=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Ignition, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_CAST)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Ignition, Condition(function Trig_Ignition_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Ignition, function Trig_Ignition_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Shalestorm Form
//
// Alternative Group Pick. Have all humans already in a group, then have it check each member for range. (more efficient)
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func001Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTerrainPathableBJ(udg_ShaleSpawnZone, PATHING_TYPE_WALKABILITY) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func002Func001002003 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( IsUnitInGroup(GetEnumUnit(), udg_AllHumansGroup) == true )
endfunction

function Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func002Func002A takes nothing returns nothing
    call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()))], udg_ShaleSpawnZone, 3.00, bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 75.00, 0.00)
    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()))], "TRIGSTR_1642")
endfunction

function Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ActiveRadarTowers >= 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func003Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), udg_MeteorStrikePoint) <= 6200.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTriggerEnabled(gg_trg_Perfect_Hearing) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func009Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTerrainPathableBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, PATHING_TYPE_FLYABILITY) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > 1
        set udg_ShaleSpawnZone=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
        set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > 2
            if ( Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
                set udg_ShaleSpawnZone=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            else
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=2
            endif
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
        endloop
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    if ( Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func002C() ) then
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocMatching(6200.00, udg_ShaleSpawnZone, Condition(function Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func002Func001002003))
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func002Func002A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func003C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func003Func001C() ) then
            call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_AlienTeam, udg_ShaleSpawnZone, 3.00, bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 75.00, 0.00)
            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, "TRIGSTR_1646")
        else
        endif
    else
    endif
    call TriggerSleepAction(5.00)
    call SetUnitPositionLoc(udg_Shalestorm, udg_ShaleSpawnZone)
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Shalestorm_Wander)
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Shalestorm_Roll_Off)
    set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
    set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > 2
        if ( Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Func009Func001C() ) then
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
            set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
        else
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=2
            call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(udg_Shalestorm, "move", udg_RandomPositionTarget)
        endif
        set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
    endloop
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Shalestorm_Form=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Shalestorm_Form)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Shalestorm_Form, function Trig_Shalestorm_Form_Actions)
endfunction

        return false

    return true

function Trig_Shalestorm_Roll_Off_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_RandomInteger=GetRandomInt(1, 9)
    if ( Trig_Shalestorm_Roll_Off_Func002C() ) then
        call SetUnitPositionLoc(udg_Shalestorm, GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Shalestorm_Hold_Zone))
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
        call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Shalestorm_Wander)
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Shalestorm_Roll_On)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function Trig_Meteors_Func004Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTerrainPathableBJ(udg_MeteorStrikePoint, PATHING_TYPE_WALKABILITY) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Meteors_Func007Func001002003 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( IsUnitInGroup(GetEnumUnit(), udg_AllHumansGroup) == true )
endfunction

function Trig_Meteors_Func007Func002A takes nothing returns nothing
    call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()))], udg_MeteorStrikePoint, 3.00, bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 100, 0.00)
    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_PlayerGroupRef[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()))], "TRIGSTR_1555")
endfunction

function Trig_Meteors_Func007C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ActiveRadarTowers >= 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Meteors_Func008Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), udg_MeteorStrikePoint) <= 2000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Meteors_Func008C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTriggerEnabled(gg_trg_Perfect_Hearing) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Meteors_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_MeteorStrikePoint=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > 1
        set udg_MeteorStrikePoint=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
        set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > 2
            if ( Trig_Meteors_Func004Func002Func001C() ) then
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
                set udg_MeteorStrikePoint=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            else
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=2
            endif
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
        endloop
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    call SetUnitPositionLocFacingLocBJ(udg_MeteorThrower, PolarProjectionBJ(udg_MeteorStrikePoint, 6000.00, GetRandomDirectionDeg()), udg_MeteorStrikePoint)
    call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(udg_MeteorThrower, "attackground", udg_MeteorStrikePoint)
    if ( Trig_Meteors_Func007C() ) then
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocMatching(2000.00, udg_MeteorStrikePoint, Condition(function Trig_Meteors_Func007Func001002003))
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Meteors_Func007Func002A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Meteors_Func008C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Meteors_Func008Func001C() ) then
            call PingMinimapLocForForceEx(udg_AlienTeam, udg_MeteorStrikePoint, 3.00, bj_MINIMAPPINGSTYLE_SIMPLE, 100.00, 100, 0.00)
            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, "TRIGSTR_1644")
        else
        endif
    else
    endif
    call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Meteor_Fire_Once)
endfunction

//===========================================================================

    set gg_trg_Meteors=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Meteors)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Meteors, 20.00)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Meteors, function Trig_Meteors_Actions)
endfunction

    return ( GetUnitTypeId(GetFilterUnit()) == 'h003' )
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Func006A takes nothing returns nothing
    call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetEnumUnit(), udg_LightningStrikeGroup)
    set udg_StaticSpireToBeStruck=GetEnumUnit()
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Func008Func003002003 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( IsUnitType(GetFilterUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_MECHANICAL) == false )
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Func008Func004Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerController(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit())) == MAP_CONTROL_USER ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) != 'n000' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Func008Func004A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Lightning_Func008Func004Func001C() ) then
        call SetUnitLifeBJ(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetEnumUnit()) - 988.00 ))
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Func008C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( CountUnitsInGroup(udg_LightningStrikeGroup) == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(udg_LightningStrikePoint, GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())) <= 7000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(udg_LightningStrikePoint, GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())) <= 6000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true

    endif
    return true

    endif
    return true

    endif
    return true

    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(udg_LightningStrikePoint, GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())) <= 2000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Func013Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(udg_LightningStrikePoint, GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())) <= 1000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Func013A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Lightning_Func013Func001C() ) then
        if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
        set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[1]
        endif
    else
        if ( Trig_Lightning_Func013Func001Func001C() ) then
            if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
            set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[2]
            endif
        else
            if ( Trig_Lightning_Func013Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
                set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[3]
                endif
            else
                if ( Trig_Lightning_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
                    set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[4]
                    endif
                else
                    if ( Trig_Lightning_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                        if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
                        set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[5]
                        endif
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Lightning_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                            if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
                            set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[6]
                            endif
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Lightning_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
                                set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[7]
                                endif
                            else
                                set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=null
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Func017C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_RandomInteger == 121 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_LightningStrikePoint=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > 1
        set udg_LightningStrikePoint=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
        set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > 2
            if ( Trig_Lightning_Func003Func002Func001C() ) then
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
                set udg_LightningStrikePoint=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            else
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=2
            endif
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
        endloop
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    call GroupClear(udg_LightningStrikeGroup)
    set udg_TempGroup=GetRandomSubGroup(1, GetUnitsInRangeOfLocMatching(300.00, udg_LightningStrikePoint, Condition(function Trig_Lightning_Func005002002003)))
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Lightning_Func006A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    if ( Trig_Lightning_Func008C() ) then
        set udg_LightningStrikePoint=GetUnitLoc(udg_StaticSpireToBeStruck)
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_LightningStrikePoint, "LightningBolt.mdx")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
    else
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_LightningStrikePoint, "LightningBolt.mdx")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocMatching(150.00, udg_LightningStrikePoint, Condition(function Trig_Lightning_Func008Func003002003))
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Lightning_Func008Func004A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    endif
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll('H005')
    call GroupAddGroup(udg_AllHumansGroup, udg_TempGroup)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Lightning_Func013A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    call PlaySoundBJ(udg_ThunderSoundToPlay)
    set udg_RandomInteger=GetRandomInt(1, 150)
    if ( Trig_Lightning_Func017C() ) then
        call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Lightning_Storm_Arrival)
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Lightning takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Lightning=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Lightning)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Lightning, 20.00)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Lightning, function Trig_Lightning_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Apocalyptic_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_LightningStrikePoint=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > 1
        set udg_LightningStrikePoint=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
        set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > 2
            if ( Trig_Lightning_Apocalyptic_Func003Func002Func001C() ) then
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
                set udg_LightningStrikePoint=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            else
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=2
            endif
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
        endloop
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    call GroupClear(udg_LightningStrikeGroup)
    set udg_TempGroup=GetRandomSubGroup(1, GetUnitsInRangeOfLocMatching(300.00, udg_LightningStrikePoint, Condition(function Trig_Lightning_Apocalyptic_Func005002002003)))
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Lightning_Apocalyptic_Func006A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    if ( Trig_Lightning_Apocalyptic_Func008C() ) then
        set udg_LightningStrikePoint=GetUnitLoc(udg_StaticSpireToBeStruck)
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_LightningStrikePoint, "LightningBolt.mdx")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
    else
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_LightningStrikePoint, "LightningBolt.mdx")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocMatching(150.00, udg_LightningStrikePoint, Condition(function Trig_Lightning_Apocalyptic_Func008Func003002003))
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Lightning_Apocalyptic_Func008Func004A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    endif
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll('H005')
    call GroupAddGroup(udg_AllHumansGroup, udg_TempGroup)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Lightning_Apocalyptic_Func013A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    call PlaySoundBJ(udg_ThunderSoundToPlay)
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func003Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTerrainPathableBJ(udg_LightningStrikePoint, PATHING_TYPE_FLYABILITY) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func005002002003 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitTypeId(GetFilterUnit()) == 'h003' )
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func006A takes nothing returns nothing
    call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetEnumUnit(), udg_LightningStrikeGroup)
    set udg_StaticSpireToBeStruck=GetEnumUnit()
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func008Func003002003 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( IsUnitType(GetFilterUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_MECHANICAL) == false )
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func008Func004Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerController(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit())) == MAP_CONTROL_USER ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) != 'n000' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func008Func004A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func008Func004Func001C() ) then
        call SetUnitLifeBJ(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetEnumUnit()) - 988.00 ))
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func008C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( CountUnitsInGroup(udg_LightningStrikeGroup) == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(udg_LightningStrikePoint, GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())) <= 7000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(udg_LightningStrikePoint, GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())) <= 6000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(udg_LightningStrikePoint, GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())) <= 5000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(udg_LightningStrikePoint, GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())) <= 4000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(udg_LightningStrikePoint, GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())) <= 3000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(udg_LightningStrikePoint, GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())) <= 2000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( DistanceBetweenPoints(udg_LightningStrikePoint, GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())) <= 1000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001C() ) then
        if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
        set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[1]
        endif
    else
        if ( Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001Func001C() ) then
            if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
            set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[2]
            endif
        else
            if ( Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
                set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[3]
                endif
            else
                if ( Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
                    set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[4]
                    endif
                else
                    if ( Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                        if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
                        set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[5]
                        endif
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                            if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
                            set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[6]
                            endif
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                if GetLocalPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) then
                                set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=udg_ThunderVariable[7]
                                endif
                            else
                                set udg_ThunderSoundToPlay=null
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_LightningStrikePoint=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > 1
        set udg_LightningStrikePoint=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
        set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > 2
            if ( Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func003Func002Func001C() ) then
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
                set udg_LightningStrikePoint=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            else
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=2
            endif
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
        endloop
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    call GroupClear(udg_LightningStrikeGroup)
    set udg_TempGroup=GetRandomSubGroup(1, GetUnitsInRangeOfLocMatching(300.00, udg_LightningStrikePoint, Condition(function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func005002002003)))
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func006A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    if ( Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func008C() ) then
        set udg_LightningStrikePoint=GetUnitLoc(udg_StaticSpireToBeStruck)
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_LightningStrikePoint, "LightningBolt.mdx")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
    else
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_LightningStrikePoint, "LightningBolt.mdx")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocMatching(135.00, udg_LightningStrikePoint, Condition(function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func008Func003002003))
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func008Func004A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    endif
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll('H005')
    call GroupAddGroup(udg_AllHumansGroup, udg_TempGroup)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Lightning_Storm_Func013A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    call PlaySoundBJ(udg_ThunderSoundToPlay)
endfunction

    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Lightning_Storm)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Lightning_Storm, 0.80)

    endif

        return false
    endif

function Trig_Ice_Geysers_Func006A takes nothing returns nothing
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(udg_IceGeyser, "frostnova", GetEnumUnit())
    if ( Trig_Ice_Geysers_Func006Func003C() ) then
        call SetUnitLifePercentBJ(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitLifePercent(GetEnumUnit()) - 20.00 ))
    else
        if ( Trig_Ice_Geysers_Func006Func003Func001C() ) then
            call SetUnitLifePercentBJ(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitLifePercent(GetEnumUnit()) - 5.00 ))
        else
        endif
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Ice_Geysers_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_IceGeyserZone=PolarProjectionBJ(GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ice_Gesyer_Origin_Zone), GetRandomReal(0.00, 2700.00), GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call SetUnitPositionLoc(udg_IceGeyser, udg_IceGeyserZone)
    call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_IceGeyserZone, "Shiva'sWrathIceAlter.mdx")
    call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(175.00, udg_IceGeyserZone)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Ice_Geysers_Func006A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
endfunction

    return true

    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Made_by_Me_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_2216")
    set udg_NumOfPlayers=12
    call CreateFogModifierRectBJ(true, Player(9), FOG_OF_WAR_VISIBLE, gg_rct_Intro_Credit_Vision)
    set udg_zRandomLetterPath="abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz"
    call VolumeGroupSetVolumeBJ(SOUND_VOLUMEGROUP_MUSIC, 75.00)
    call SetDayNightModels("", "")
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'hgry', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), GetUnitLoc(gg_unit_hgry_0031), 180.00)
    set udg_CreditUnit[1]=GetLastCreatedUnit()
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'hgyr', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), GetUnitLoc(gg_unit_hgyr_0030), 180.00)
    set udg_CreditUnit[2]=GetLastCreatedUnit()
    call RemoveUnit(gg_unit_hgyr_0030)
    call RemoveUnit(gg_unit_hgry_0031)
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > udg_NumOfPlayers
        if ( (true) ) then // INLINED!!
            call CameraSetupApplyForPlayer(true, gg_cam_IntroCam, ConvertedPlayer(udg_GenericLoopCount), 0)
            call CreateFogModifierRectBJ(true, ConvertedPlayer(udg_GenericLoopCount), FOG_OF_WAR_VISIBLE, gg_rct_Intro_Credit_Vision)
        else
        endif
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    call DialogSetMessageBJ(udg_PreferenceMenu, ( "Choose a preference or wait: " + I2S(udg_WaitTimeToChooseRace) ))
    call DialogSetMessageBJ(udg_DestroyBuildingMenu, "TRIGSTR_1572")
    call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_PreferenceMenu, "TRIGSTR_1168")
    set udg_MenuButtons[1]=GetLastCreatedButtonBJ()
    call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_PreferenceMenu, "TRIGSTR_1169")
    set udg_MenuButtons[0]=GetLastCreatedButtonBJ()
    call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_DestroyBuildingMenu, "TRIGSTR_1570")
    set udg_MenuButtons[3]=GetLastCreatedButtonBJ()
    call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_DestroyBuildingMenu, "TRIGSTR_1571")
    set udg_MenuButtons[4]=GetLastCreatedButtonBJ()
    call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_EndGameStatsMenu, "TRIGSTR_1667")
    set udg_MenuButtons[5]=GetLastCreatedButtonBJ()
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > udg_NumOfPlayers
        if ( (true) ) then // INLINED!!
            call DialogDisplayBJ(true, udg_PreferenceMenu, ConvertedPlayer(udg_GenericLoopCount))
        else
        endif
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function Trig_First_Func004Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_First_Func006Func002002001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetPlayerSlotState(GetFilterPlayer()) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING )
endfunction

function Trig_First_Func006C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_aPlayerChoseAlien == "yes" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_First_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call RemoveUnit(gg_unit_h00G_0106)
    call RemoveUnit(gg_unit_hgry_0031)
    set udg_NumOfPlayers=12
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > udg_NumOfPlayers
        if ( (true) ) then // INLINED!!
            call CameraSetupApplyForPlayer(true, gg_cam_Default, ConvertedPlayer(udg_GenericLoopCount), 0)
        else
        endif
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    call CreateFogModifierRadiusLocBJ(true, udg_AlienPlayer, FOG_OF_WAR_VISIBLE, GetRectCenter(gg_rct_AutoViewLava), 130.00)
    if ( Trig_First_Func006C() ) then
        set udg_AlienPlayer=ForcePickRandomPlayer(udg_DesireToBeAlien)
    else
        set udg_AlienPlayer=ForcePickRandomPlayer(GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_First_Func006Func002002001001)))
    endif
    call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A061', udg_AlienPlayer)
    set udg_AlienTeam=GetForceOfPlayer(udg_AlienPlayer)
    call SetForceAllianceStateBJ(udg_AlienTeam, GetPlayersByMapControl(MAP_CONTROL_USER), bj_ALLIANCE_UNALLIED)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'H005', udg_AlienPlayer, GetUnitLoc(GroupPickRandomUnit(GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll('ewsp'))), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(GetLastCreatedUnit(), udg_AlienPlayer)
    set udg_AlienUnit=GetLastCreatedUnit()
    call ShowUnitHide(udg_AlienUnit)
    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, "TRIGSTR_2215")
    call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A07C', udg_AlienPlayer)
    call SetUnitManaBJ(udg_AlienUnit, 0)
    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('I00V', udg_AlienUnit)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n007', udg_AlienPlayer, GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_PredatorNest=GetLastCreatedUnit()
    if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(), udg_AlienTeam) then
    set udg_AlienLightVar="AlienLight.mdx"
    set udg_HeartBeatVariable=gg_snd_HeartBeat
    call VolumeGroupSetVolumeBJ(SOUND_VOLUMEGROUP_UI, 0.00)
    endif
    call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", udg_AlienUnit, udg_AlienLightVar)
    call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(udg_AlienPlayer, GetUnitLoc(GetLastCreatedUnit()), 0)
    call ConditionalTriggerExecute(gg_trg_Second)
endfunction

    set gg_trg_First=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventSingle(gg_trg_First, 10.00)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_First, function Trig_First_Actions)
endfunction

    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Second_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_NumOfPlayers=12
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > udg_NumOfPlayers
        if ( (true) ) then // INLINED!!
            call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(udg_AlienPlayer, ConvertedPlayer(udg_GenericLoopCount), bj_ALLIANCE_UNALLIED)
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
            loop
                exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > udg_NumOfPlayers
                call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(ConvertedPlayer(udg_GenericLoopCount), ConvertedPlayer(udg_GenericSubLoopCount), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED_VISION)
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
            endloop
        else
        endif
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    call ConditionalTriggerExecute(gg_trg_Third)
endfunction

function Trig_Third_Func002Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetPlayerSlotState(ConvertedPlayer(udg_xSpawnNumberLoop)) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Third_Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( ConvertedPlayer(udg_xSpawnNumberLoop) != udg_AlienPlayer ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Third_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_NumOfPlayers=12
    set udg_xSpawnNumberLoop=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_xSpawnNumberLoop > udg_NumOfPlayers
        if ( Trig_Third_Func002Func001C() ) then
            if ( Trig_Third_Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(udg_AlienPlayer, ConvertedPlayer(udg_xSpawnNumberLoop), bj_ALLIANCE_UNALLIED)
                call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(ConvertedPlayer(udg_xSpawnNumberLoop), udg_AlienPlayer, bj_ALLIANCE_UNALLIED)
                call CreateFogModifierRadiusLocBJ(true, ConvertedPlayer(udg_xSpawnNumberLoop), FOG_OF_WAR_VISIBLE, GetRectCenter(gg_rct_AutoViewLava), 130.00)
                set udg_SelectedSpawnNode=GroupPickRandomUnit(GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll('osp1'))
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'H004', ConvertedPlayer(udg_xSpawnNumberLoop), GetUnitLoc(udg_SelectedSpawnNode), bj_UNIT_FACING)
                call RemoveUnit(udg_SelectedSpawnNode)
                set udg_HumansTotal=( udg_HumansTotal + 1 )
                set udg_PlayerUnitMatch[udg_xSpawnNumberLoop]=GetLastCreatedUnit()
                call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetLastCreatedUnit(), udg_AllHumansGroup)
                call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(GetLastCreatedUnit(), ConvertedPlayer(udg_xSpawnNumberLoop))
                call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(ConvertedPlayer(udg_xSpawnNumberLoop), GetUnitLoc(GetLastCreatedUnit()), 0)
                set udg_RandomInteger=GetRandomInt(1, 3)
                if ( (udg_RandomInteger == 2) ) then // INLINED!!
                    call CreateItemLoc('I007', GetUnitLoc(GetLastCreatedUnit()))
                else
                    // n
                endif
                if ( (udg_RandomInteger == 1) ) then // INLINED!!
                    call CreateItemLoc('I000', GetUnitLoc(GetLastCreatedUnit()))
                else
                    // n
                endif
                if ( (udg_RandomInteger == 3) ) then // INLINED!!
                    call CreateItemLoc('I002', GetUnitLoc(GetLastCreatedUnit()))
                else
                    // n
                endif
                if ( (udg_RandomInteger == 3) ) then // INLINED!!
                    call SetItemCharges(GetLastCreatedItem(), 1)
                else
                    // n
                endif
                call IssueTargetItemOrder(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "smart", GetLastCreatedItem())
                call SetUnitLifePercentBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), 10.00)
                call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A00S', ConvertedPlayer(udg_xSpawnNumberLoop))
                call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A04A', ConvertedPlayer(udg_xSpawnNumberLoop))
                call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A05K', ConvertedPlayer(udg_xSpawnNumberLoop))
            else
                set udg_SelectedSpawnNode=GroupPickRandomUnit(GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll('osp1'))
                set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetUnitLoc(udg_SelectedSpawnNode)
                call RemoveUnit(udg_SelectedSpawnNode)
                set udg_RandomInteger=GetRandomInt(1, 5)
                if ( (udg_RandomInteger == 1) ) then // INLINED!!
                    call CreateItemLoc('I000', udg_RandomPositionTarget)
                else
                    // n
                endif
                if ( (udg_RandomInteger == 2) ) then // INLINED!!
                    call CreateItemLoc('I007', udg_RandomPositionTarget)
                else
                    // n
                endif
                if ( (udg_RandomInteger == 3) ) then // INLINED!!
                    call CreateItemLoc('I002', udg_RandomPositionTarget)
                else
                    // n
                endif
                if ( (udg_RandomInteger == 3) ) then // INLINED!!
                    call SetItemCharges(GetLastCreatedItem(), 1)
                else
                    // n
                endif
                if ( (udg_RandomInteger == 4) ) then // INLINED!!
                    call CreateItemLoc('I00S', udg_RandomPositionTarget)
                else
                    // n
                endif
                if ( (udg_RandomInteger == 5) ) then // INLINED!!
                    call CreateItemLoc('I00R', udg_RandomPositionTarget)
                else
                    // n
                endif
                call CreatePermanentCorpseLocBJ(bj_CORPSETYPE_FLESH, 'H004', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_RandomPositionTarget, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            endif
        else
        endif
        set udg_xSpawnNumberLoop=udg_xSpawnNumberLoop + 1
    endloop
    call ConditionalTriggerExecute(gg_trg_Fourth)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Third takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Third=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Third)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Third, function Trig_Third_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Fourth
//
// Put Aura spells into Spellbook to hide them. Put Cooldown on Nano-Repair.
// Remove use of Integer A?
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Fourth_Func001002 takes nothing returns nothing
    call RemoveUnit(GetEnumUnit())
endfunction

function Trig_Fourth_Func002002 takes nothing returns nothing
    call RemoveUnit(GetEnumUnit())
endfunction

function Trig_Fourth_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll('ewsp'), function Trig_Fourth_Func001002)
    call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll('osp1'), function Trig_Fourth_Func002002)
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Player_Initial_Healing)
    call EnableWorldFogBoundaryBJ(false, GetPlayersAll())
    call PlaySoundBJ(gg_snd_LazarusSystem)
    set udg_RandomReal=100.00
    if IsPlayerInForce(GetLocalPlayer(), udg_AlienTeam) then
    set udg_RandomReal=0.00
    endif
    call SetSoundVolumeBJ(GetLastPlayedSound(), udg_RandomReal)
    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_2220")
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Fourth takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Fourth=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Fourth)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Fourth, function Trig_Fourth_Actions)
endfunction

    if ( not ( udg_AlienTotalAbilitiesLearned <= 4 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_AlienTotalAbilitiesLearned <= 5 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A02G', udg_AlienUnit)
    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, "TRIGSTR_1234")
    set udg_AlienTotalAbilitiesLearned=( udg_AlienTotalAbilitiesLearned + 1 )
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Menu Countdown
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Menu_Countdown_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_WaitTimeToChooseRace == 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Menu_Countdown_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_WaitTimeToChooseRace=( udg_WaitTimeToChooseRace - 1 )
    call DialogSetMessageBJ(udg_PreferenceMenu, ( "Choose a preference or wait: " + I2S(udg_WaitTimeToChooseRace) ))
    if ( Trig_Menu_Countdown_Func004C() ) then
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > udg_NumOfPlayers
            call DialogDisplayBJ(false, udg_PreferenceMenu, ConvertedPlayer(udg_GenericLoopCount))
            set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
        endloop
    else
    endif
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Menu_Countdown=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Menu_Countdown, 1.00)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Menu_Countdown, function Trig_Menu_Countdown_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Alien Spawning
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Alien_Spawning_Func003Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTerrainPathableBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, PATHING_TYPE_WALKABILITY) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Alien_Spawning_Func004Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTerrainPathableBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, PATHING_TYPE_WALKABILITY) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Alien_Spawning_Func005Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTerrainPathableBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, PATHING_TYPE_WALKABILITY) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Alien_Spawning_Func006Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTerrainPathableBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, PATHING_TYPE_WALKABILITY) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Alien_Spawning_Func007Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsTerrainPathableBJ(udg_RandomPositionTarget, PATHING_TYPE_WALKABILITY) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Alien_Spawning_Func010Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Alien_Spawning_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A05I', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE))
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > 51
        set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
        set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > 2
            if ( Trig_Alien_Spawning_Func003Func002Func001C() ) then
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
                set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            else
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=2
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n001', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_RandomPositionTarget, bj_UNIT_FACING)
                call SetUnitColor(GetLastCreatedUnit(), GetPlayerColor(ConvertedPlayer(GetRandomInt(1, 13))))
            endif
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
        endloop
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > 12
        set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
        set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > 2
            if ( Trig_Alien_Spawning_Func004Func002Func001C() ) then
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
                set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            else
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=2
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n003', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_RandomPositionTarget, bj_UNIT_FACING)
            endif
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
        endloop
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > 5
        set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
        set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > 2
            if ( Trig_Alien_Spawning_Func005Func002Func001C() ) then
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
                set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            else
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=2
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(2, 'n002', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_RandomPositionTarget, bj_UNIT_FACING)
            endif
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
        endloop
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > 5
        set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
        set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > 2
            if ( Trig_Alien_Spawning_Func006Func002Func001C() ) then
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
                set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            else
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=2
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n005', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_RandomPositionTarget, bj_UNIT_FACING)
            endif
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
        endloop
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    set udg_GenericLoopCount=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_GenericLoopCount > 1
        set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
        set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
        loop
            exitwhen udg_GenericSubLoopCount > 2
            if ( Trig_Alien_Spawning_Func007Func002Func001C() ) then
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=1
                set udg_RandomPositionTarget=GetRandomLocInRect(GetPlayableMapRect())
            else
                set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=2
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n004', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_RandomPositionTarget, bj_UNIT_FACING)
                set udg_HydraUnit=GetLastCreatedUnit()
            endif
            set udg_GenericSubLoopCount=udg_GenericSubLoopCount + 1
        endloop
        set udg_GenericLoopCount=udg_GenericLoopCount + 1
    endloop
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'o004', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), GetRectCenter(GetPlayableMapRect()), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_MeteorThrower=GetLastCreatedUnit()
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=12
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( (true) ) then // INLINED!!
            call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(Player(21), ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), bj_ALLIANCE_UNALLIED)
        else
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'h008', Player(21), GetRectCenter(GetPlayableMapRect()), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_IceGeyser=GetLastCreatedUnit()
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Alien_Spawning takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Alien_Spawning=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventSingle(gg_trg_Alien_Spawning, 0.03)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Alien_Spawning, function Trig_Alien_Spawning_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Speed Upgrade
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Speed_Upgrade_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A07B' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Speed_Upgrade_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DisplayTimedTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, 2.00, "TRIGSTR_2193")
    call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('S005', udg_AlienUnit, ( GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('S005', udg_AlienUnit) + 1 ))
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Speed_Upgrade takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Speed_Upgrade=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Speed_Upgrade, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Speed_Upgrade, Condition(function Trig_Speed_Upgrade_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Speed_Upgrade, function Trig_Speed_Upgrade_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Damage Upgrade
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Damage_Upgrade_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A07A' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Damage_Upgrade_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DisplayTimedTextToForce(udg_AlienTeam, 2.00, "TRIGSTR_2194")
    call BlzSetUnitBaseDamage(udg_AlienUnit, ( BlzGetUnitBaseDamage(udg_AlienUnit, 0) + 10 ), 0)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Skraaglings
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Skraaglings_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A07D' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Skraaglings_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'u005', udg_AlienPlayer, GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(60, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "smart", udg_AlienUnit)
    call SetUnitColor(GetLastCreatedUnit(), PLAYER_COLOR_COAL)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'u005', udg_AlienPlayer, GetUnitLoc(udg_AlienUnit), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(60, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "smart", udg_AlienUnit)
    call SetUnitColor(GetLastCreatedUnit(), PLAYER_COLOR_COAL)
endfunction

function InitCustomPlayerSlots takes nothing returns nothing

    // Player 0
    call SetPlayerStartLocation(Player(0), 0)
    call SetPlayerColor(Player(0), ConvertPlayerColor(0))
    call SetPlayerRacePreference(Player(0), RACE_PREF_HUMAN)
    call SetPlayerRaceSelectable(Player(0), false)
    call SetPlayerController(Player(0), MAP_CONTROL_USER)

    // Player 1
    call SetPlayerStartLocation(Player(1), 1)
    call SetPlayerColor(Player(1), ConvertPlayerColor(1))
    call SetPlayerRacePreference(Player(1), RACE_PREF_HUMAN)
    call SetPlayerRaceSelectable(Player(1), false)
    call SetPlayerController(Player(1), MAP_CONTROL_USER)

    // Player 2
    call SetPlayerStartLocation(Player(2), 2)
    call SetPlayerColor(Player(2), ConvertPlayerColor(2))
    call SetPlayerRacePreference(Player(2), RACE_PREF_HUMAN)
    call SetPlayerRaceSelectable(Player(2), false)
    call SetPlayerController(Player(2), MAP_CONTROL_USER)

    // Player 3
    call SetPlayerStartLocation(Player(3), 3)
    call SetPlayerColor(Player(3), ConvertPlayerColor(3))
    call SetPlayerRacePreference(Player(3), RACE_PREF_HUMAN)
    call SetPlayerRaceSelectable(Player(3), false)
    call SetPlayerController(Player(3), MAP_CONTROL_USER)

    // Player 4
    call SetPlayerStartLocation(Player(4), 4)
    call SetPlayerColor(Player(4), ConvertPlayerColor(4))
    call SetPlayerRacePreference(Player(4), RACE_PREF_HUMAN)
    call SetPlayerRaceSelectable(Player(4), false)
    call SetPlayerController(Player(4), MAP_CONTROL_USER)

    // Player 5
    call SetPlayerStartLocation(Player(5), 5)
    call SetPlayerColor(Player(5), ConvertPlayerColor(5))
    call SetPlayerRacePreference(Player(5), RACE_PREF_HUMAN)
    call SetPlayerRaceSelectable(Player(5), false)
    call SetPlayerController(Player(5), MAP_CONTROL_USER)

    // Player 6
    call SetPlayerStartLocation(Player(6), 6)
    call SetPlayerColor(Player(6), ConvertPlayerColor(6))
    call SetPlayerRacePreference(Player(6), RACE_PREF_HUMAN)
    call SetPlayerRaceSelectable(Player(6), false)
    call SetPlayerController(Player(6), MAP_CONTROL_USER)

    // Player 7
    call SetPlayerStartLocation(Player(7), 7)
    call SetPlayerColor(Player(7), ConvertPlayerColor(7))
    call SetPlayerRacePreference(Player(7), RACE_PREF_HUMAN)
    call SetPlayerRaceSelectable(Player(7), false)
    call SetPlayerController(Player(7), MAP_CONTROL_USER)

    // Player 8
    call SetPlayerStartLocation(Player(8), 8)
    call SetPlayerColor(Player(8), ConvertPlayerColor(8))
    call SetPlayerRacePreference(Player(8), RACE_PREF_HUMAN)
    call SetPlayerRaceSelectable(Player(8), false)
    call SetPlayerController(Player(8), MAP_CONTROL_USER)

    // Player 9
    call SetPlayerStartLocation(Player(9), 9)
    call SetPlayerColor(Player(9), ConvertPlayerColor(9))
    call SetPlayerRacePreference(Player(9), RACE_PREF_HUMAN)
    call SetPlayerRaceSelectable(Player(9), false)
    call SetPlayerController(Player(9), MAP_CONTROL_USER)

endfunction

function InitCustomTeams takes nothing returns nothing
    // Force: TRIGSTR_1720
    call SetPlayerTeam(Player(0), 0)
    call SetPlayerTeam(Player(1), 0)
    call SetPlayerTeam(Player(2), 0)
    call SetPlayerTeam(Player(3), 0)
    call SetPlayerTeam(Player(4), 0)
    call SetPlayerTeam(Player(5), 0)
    call SetPlayerTeam(Player(6), 0)
    call SetPlayerTeam(Player(7), 0)
    call SetPlayerTeam(Player(8), 0)

    // Force: TRIGSTR_2128
    call SetPlayerTeam(Player(9), 1)

endfunction

function InitAllyPriorities takes nothing returns nothing

    call SetStartLocPrioCount(0, 2)
    call SetStartLocPrio(0, 0, 2, MAP_LOC_PRIO_LOW)
    call SetStartLocPrio(0, 1, 4, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)

    call SetStartLocPrioCount(1, 1)
    call SetStartLocPrio(1, 0, 8, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)

    call SetStartLocPrioCount(2, 1)
    call SetStartLocPrio(2, 0, 4, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)

    call SetStartLocPrioCount(3, 3)
    call SetStartLocPrio(3, 0, 0, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)
    call SetStartLocPrio(3, 1, 5, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)
    call SetStartLocPrio(3, 2, 8, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)

    call SetStartLocPrioCount(4, 2)
    call SetStartLocPrio(4, 0, 0, MAP_LOC_PRIO_LOW)
    call SetStartLocPrio(4, 1, 2, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)

    call SetStartLocPrioCount(5, 3)
    call SetStartLocPrio(5, 0, 0, MAP_LOC_PRIO_LOW)
    call SetStartLocPrio(5, 1, 2, MAP_LOC_PRIO_LOW)
    call SetStartLocPrio(5, 2, 3, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)

    call SetStartLocPrioCount(6, 2)
    call SetStartLocPrio(6, 0, 1, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)
    call SetStartLocPrio(6, 1, 9, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)

    call SetStartLocPrioCount(7, 2)
    call SetStartLocPrio(7, 0, 4, MAP_LOC_PRIO_LOW)
    call SetStartLocPrio(7, 1, 9, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)

    call SetStartLocPrioCount(8, 1)
    call SetStartLocPrio(8, 0, 1, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)

    call SetStartLocPrioCount(9, 3)
    call SetStartLocPrio(9, 0, 4, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)
    call SetStartLocPrio(9, 1, 6, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)
    call SetStartLocPrio(9, 2, 7, MAP_LOC_PRIO_HIGH)
endfunction

//***************************************************************************
//*
//*  Main Initialization
//*
//***************************************************************************

//===========================================================================
function main takes nothing returns nothing
    local weathereffect we
    call SetCameraBounds(- 17152.0 + GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_LEFT), 2560.0 + GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_BOTTOM), 5888.0 - GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_RIGHT), 29696.0 - GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_TOP), - 17152.0 + GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_LEFT), 29696.0 - GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_TOP), 5888.0 - GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_RIGHT), 2560.0 + GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_BOTTOM))
    call SetDayNightModels("Environment\\DNC\\DNCAshenvale\\DNCAshenvaleTerrain\\DNCAshenvaleTerrain.mdl", "Environment\\DNC\\DNCAshenvale\\DNCAshenvaleUnit\\DNCAshenvaleUnit.mdl")
    set we=AddWeatherEffect(Rect(- 17920.0, - 2048.0, 6656.0, 30720.0), 'SNls')
    call EnableWeatherEffect(we, true)
    call NewSoundEnvironment("Default")
    call SetAmbientDaySound("AshenvaleDay")
    call SetAmbientNightSound("AshenvaleNight")
    call SetMapMusic("Music", true, 0)
    call InitSounds()
    call CreateRegions()
    call CreateCameras()
    call CreateAllDestructables()
    call CreateAllUnits()
    call InitBlizzard()


    call InitGlobals()
    call InitCustomTriggers()
    call ConditionalTriggerExecute(gg_trg_Melee_Initialization) // INLINED!!

endfunction

//***************************************************************************
//*
//*  Map Configuration
//*
//***************************************************************************

function config takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetMapName("TRIGSTR_003")
    call SetMapDescription("TRIGSTR_005")
    call SetPlayers(10)
    call SetTeams(10)
    call SetGamePlacement(MAP_PLACEMENT_TEAMS_TOGETHER)

    call DefineStartLocation(0, - 4352.0, 17088.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(1, - 1088.0, 11008.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(2, - 9024.0, 19328.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(3, 896.0, 20608.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(4, - 7808.0, 17152.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(5, - 3264.0, 23808.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(6, - 5696.0, 8192.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(7, - 13248.0, 13568.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(8, 768.0, 14080.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(9, - 8960.0, 11968.0)

    // Player setup
    call InitCustomPlayerSlots()
    call InitCustomTeams()
    call InitAllyPriorities()
endfunction
